## Analytics

 *Analytics platforms, SDK's, error tracking and real-time answers about your app*

- [Answers by Fabric](https://get.fabric.io) - Answers gives you real-time insight into people’s experience in your app.
- [Aptabase](https://aptabase.com/for-swift) - Open Source, Privacy-First and Simple Analytics for Swift Apps.
- [Bugsnag](https://www.bugsnag.com/platforms/ios-crash-reporting) - Error tracking with a free tier. Error reports include data on device, release, user, and allows arbitrary data.
- [Countly](https://count.ly) - Open source, mobile & web analytics, crash reports and push notifications platform for iOS & Android.
- [devtodev](https://www.devtodev.com/) - Comprehensive analytics service that improves your project and saves time for product development.
- [Embrace](http://embrace.io) - Mobile observability, built on OpenTelemetry, to provide user-focused, reliable apps.
- [Emerge Tools](https://www.emergetools.com) - Prevent app size & performance regressions on every pull request, get automated insights on how to improve.
- [Instabug](https://instabug.com) - In-app feedback, Bug and Crash reporting, Fix Bugs Faster through user-steps, video recordings, screen annotation, network requests logging.
- [Matomo](https://github.com/matomo-org/matomo-sdk-ios) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/matomo-org/matomo-sdk-ios?style=flat)](https://github.com/matomo-org/matomo-sdk-ios/stargazers) - The MatomoTracker is an iOS, tvOS and macOS SDK for sending app analytics to a Matomo server.
- [Measure](https://measure.sh/) - Open source, self-hostable mobile app monitoring with error tracking, performance tracing and full session timelines to spend less time stitching context and fix issues faster.
- [Mixpanel](https://mixpanel.com/) - Advanced analytics platform.
- [MOCA Analytics](https://www.mocaplatform.com/features) - Paid cross-platform analytics backend.
- [Segment](https://github.com/segmentio/analytics-ios) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/segmentio/analytics-ios?style=flat)](https://github.com/segmentio/analytics-ios/stargazers) - The hassle-free way to integrate analytics into any iOS application.
- [Sentry](https://sentry.io/) - Sentry provides self-hosted and cloud-based error monitoring that helps all software teams discover, triage, and prioritize errors in real-time.
- [Shake](https://www.shakebugs.com/) - In-app feedback and bug reporting tool. Fix app bugs up to 50x faster with detailed device data, repro steps, video recording, black box data, network requests and custom logging.

**[back to top](#contributing-and-collaborating)**

## App Routing

  *Elegant URL routing, navigation frameworks, deep links and more*

- [ApplicationCoordinator](https://github.com/AndreyPanov/ApplicationCoordinator) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/AndreyPanov/ApplicationCoordinator?style=flat)](https://github.com/AndreyPanov/ApplicationCoordinator/stargazers) - Coordinator is an object that handles navigation flow and shares flow’s handling for the next coordinator after switching on the next chain.
- [Appz](https://github.com/SwiftKitz/Appz) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/SwiftKitz/Appz?style=flat)](https://github.com/SwiftKitz/Appz/stargazers) - Easily launch and deeplink into external applications, falling back to web if not installed.
- [Composable Navigator](https://github.com/Bahn-X/swift-composable-navigator) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/Bahn-X/swift-composable-navigator?style=flat)](https://github.com/Bahn-X/swift-composable-navigator/stargazers) - An open source library for building deep-linkable SwiftUI applications with composition, testing and ergonomics in mind
- [Crossroad](https://github.com/giginet/Crossroad) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/giginet/Crossroad?style=flat)](https://github.com/giginet/Crossroad/stargazers) - Crossroad is an URL router focused on handling Custom URL Schemes. Using this, you can route multiple URL schemes and fetch arguments and parameters easily.
- [DeepLinkKit](https://github.com/button/DeepLinkKit) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/button/DeepLinkKit?style=flat)](https://github.com/button/DeepLinkKit/stargazers) - A splendid route-matching, block-based way to handle your deep links.
- [JLRoutes](https://github.com/joeldev/JLRoutes) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/joeldev/JLRoutes?style=flat)](https://github.com/joeldev/JLRoutes/stargazers) - URL routing library for iOS with a simple block-based API.
- [Linker](https://github.com/MaksimKurpa/Linker) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/MaksimKurpa/Linker?style=flat)](https://github.com/MaksimKurpa/Linker/stargazers) - Lightweight way to handle internal and external deeplinks for iOS.
- [Marshroute](https://github.com/avito-tech/Marshroute) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/avito-tech/Marshroute?style=flat)](https://github.com/avito-tech/Marshroute/stargazers) - Marshroute is an iOS Library for making your Routers simple but extremely powerful.
- [RouteComposer](https://github.com/ekazaev/route-composer) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/ekazaev/route-composer?style=flat)](https://github.com/ekazaev/route-composer/stargazers) - Library that helps to handle view controllers composition, routing and deeplinking tasks.
- [RxFlow](https://github.com/RxSwiftCommunity/RxFlow) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/RxSwiftCommunity/RxFlow?style=flat)](https://github.com/RxSwiftCommunity/RxFlow/stargazers) - Navigation framework for iOS applications based on a Reactive Flow Coordinator pattern.
- [SwiftCurrent](https://github.com/wwt/SwiftCurrent) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/wwt/SwiftCurrent?style=flat)](https://github.com/wwt/SwiftCurrent/stargazers) - A library for managing complex workflows.
- [SwiftRouter](https://github.com/skyline75489/SwiftRouter) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/skyline75489/SwiftRouter?style=flat)](https://github.com/skyline75489/SwiftRouter/stargazers) - A URL Router for iOS.
- [URLNavigator](https://github.com/devxoul/URLNavigator) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/devxoul/URLNavigator?style=flat)](https://github.com/devxoul/URLNavigator/stargazers) - Elegant URL Routing for Swift
- [WAAppRouting](https://github.com/Wasappli/WAAppRouting) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/Wasappli/WAAppRouting?style=flat)](https://github.com/Wasappli/WAAppRouting/stargazers) - iOS routing done right. Handles both URL recognition and controller displaying with parsed parameters. All in one line, controller stack preserved automatically!

**[back to top](#contributing-and-collaborating)**

## App Store

*Apple Guidelines and version notification libraries*

- [Apple Review Guidelines](https://developer.apple.com/app-store/review/#common-app-rejections) - Highlighted some of the most common issues that cause apps to get rejected.
- [Free App Store Optimization Tool](https://www.mobileaction.co) - Lets you track your App Store visibility in terms of keywords and competitors.

**[back to top](#contributing-and-collaborating)**

## Apple TV

*tvOS view controllers, wrappers, template managers and video players.*

- [ParallaxView](https://github.com/PGSSoft/ParallaxView) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/PGSSoft/ParallaxView?style=flat)](https://github.com/PGSSoft/ParallaxView/stargazers) - iOS controls and extensions that add parallax effect to your application.
- [TvOSPinKeyboard](https://github.com/zattoo/TvOSPinKeyboard) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/zattoo/TvOSPinKeyboard?style=flat)](https://github.com/zattoo/TvOSPinKeyboard/stargazers) - PIN keyboard for tvOS.
- [XCDYouTubeKit](https://github.com/0xced/XCDYouTubeKit) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/0xced/XCDYouTubeKit?style=flat)](https://github.com/0xced/XCDYouTubeKit/stargazers) - YouTube video player for iOS, tvOS and macOS.

**[back to top](#contributing-and-collaborating)**

## Architecture Patterns

*Clean architecture, Viper, MVVM, Reactive... choose your weapon.*

- [Clean Architecture for SwiftUI + Combine](https://github.com/nalexn/clean-architecture-swiftui) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/nalexn/clean-architecture-swiftui?style=flat)](https://github.com/nalexn/clean-architecture-swiftui/stargazers) - A demo project showcasing the production setup of the SwiftUI app with Clean Architecture.
- [CleanArchitectureRxSwift](https://github.com/sergdort/CleanArchitectureRxSwift) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/sergdort/CleanArchitectureRxSwift?style=flat)](https://github.com/sergdort/CleanArchitectureRxSwift/stargazers) - Example of Clean Architecture of iOS app using RxSwift.
- [ios-architecture](https://github.com/tailec/ios-architecture) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/tailec/ios-architecture?style=flat)](https://github.com/tailec/ios-architecture/stargazers) - A collection of iOS architectures - MVC, MVVM, MVVM+RxSwift, VIPER, RIBs and many others.
- [iOS-Viper-Architecture](https://github.com/MindorksOpenSource/iOS-Viper-Architecture) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/MindorksOpenSource/iOS-Viper-Architecture?style=flat)](https://github.com/MindorksOpenSource/iOS-Viper-Architecture/stargazers) - This repository contains a detailed sample app that implements VIPER architecture in iOS using libraries and frameworks like Alamofire, AlamofireImage, PKHUD, CoreData etc.
- [Reactant](https://github.com/Brightify/Reactant) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/Brightify/Reactant?style=flat)](https://github.com/Brightify/Reactant/stargazers) - Reactant is a reactive architecture for iOS.
- [Spin](https://github.com/Spinners/Spin.Swift) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/Spinners/Spin.Swift?style=flat)](https://github.com/Spinners/Spin.Swift/stargazers) - A universal implementation of a Feedback Loop system for RxSwift, ReactiveSwift and Combine
- [SwiftyVIPER](https://github.com/codytwinton/SwiftyVIPER) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/codytwinton/SwiftyVIPER?style=flat)](https://github.com/codytwinton/SwiftyVIPER/stargazers) - Makes implementing VIPER architecture much easier and cleaner.
- [The Composable Architecture](https://github.com/pointfreeco/swift-composable-architecture) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/pointfreeco/swift-composable-architecture?style=flat)](https://github.com/pointfreeco/swift-composable-architecture/stargazers) - The Composable Architecture is a library for building applications in a consistent and understandable way, with composition, testing, and ergonomics in mind.
- [Viperit](https://github.com/ferranabello/Viperit) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/ferranabello/Viperit?style=flat)](https://github.com/ferranabello/Viperit/stargazers) - Viper Framework for iOS. Develop an app following VIPER architecture in an easy way. Written and tested in Swift.

**[back to top](#contributing-and-collaborating)**

## ARKit

*Library and tools to help you build unparalleled augmented reality experiences*

- [ARKit Virtual Objects](https://github.com/ignacio-chiazzo/ARKit) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/ignacio-chiazzo/ARKit?style=flat)](https://github.com/ignacio-chiazzo/ARKit/stargazers) - Placing Virtual Objects in Augmented Reality.
- [ARKit-CoreLocation](https://github.com/ProjectDent/ARKit-CoreLocation) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/ProjectDent/ARKit-CoreLocation?style=flat)](https://github.com/ProjectDent/ARKit-CoreLocation/stargazers) - Combines the high accuracy of AR with the scale of GPS data.
- [ARVideoKit](https://github.com/AFathi/ARVideoKit) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/AFathi/ARVideoKit?style=flat)](https://github.com/AFathi/ARVideoKit/stargazers) - Record and capture ARKit videos, photos, Live Photos, and GIFs.
- [SmileToUnlock](https://github.com/rsrbk/SmileToUnlock) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/rsrbk/SmileToUnlock?style=flat)](https://github.com/rsrbk/SmileToUnlock/stargazers) - This library uses ARKit Face Tracking in order to catch a user's smile.

**[back to top](#contributing-and-collaborating)**

## Authentication

*Oauth and Oauth2 libraries, social logins and captcha tools.*

- [Heimdallr.swift](https://github.com/trivago/Heimdallr.swift) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/trivago/Heimdallr.swift?style=flat)](https://github.com/trivago/Heimdallr.swift/stargazers) - Easy to use OAuth 2 library for iOS, written in Swift.
- [OAuth2](https://github.com/p2/OAuth2) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/p2/OAuth2?style=flat)](https://github.com/p2/OAuth2/stargazers) - OAuth2 framework for macOS and iOS, written in Swift.
- [OAuthSwift](https://github.com/OAuthSwift/OAuthSwift) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/OAuthSwift/OAuthSwift?style=flat)](https://github.com/OAuthSwift/OAuthSwift/stargazers) - Swift based OAuth library for iOS
- [ReCaptcha](https://github.com/fjcaetano/ReCaptcha) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/fjcaetano/ReCaptcha?style=flat)](https://github.com/fjcaetano/ReCaptcha/stargazers) - (In)visible ReCaptcha for iOS.
- [SwiftyOAuth](https://github.com/delba/SwiftyOAuth) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/delba/SwiftyOAuth?style=flat)](https://github.com/delba/SwiftyOAuth/stargazers) - A simple OAuth library for iOS with a built-in set of providers.

**[back to top](#contributing-and-collaborating)**

## Blockchain

*Tool for smart contract interactions. Bitcoin protocol implementations and Frameworks for interacting with cryptocurrencies.*

- [BitcoinKit](https://github.com/yenom/BitcoinKit) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/yenom/BitcoinKit?style=flat)](https://github.com/yenom/BitcoinKit/stargazers) - Bitcoin protocol toolkit for Swift, BitcoinKit implements Bitcoin protocol in Swift. It is an implementation of the Bitcoin SPV protocol written in swift.
- [EthereumKit](https://github.com/yuzushioh/EthereumKit) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/yuzushioh/EthereumKit?style=flat)](https://github.com/yuzushioh/EthereumKit/stargazers) - EthereumKit is a free, open-source Swift framework for easily interacting with the Ethereum.
- [Web3.swift](https://github.com/Boilertalk/Web3.swift) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/Boilertalk/Web3.swift?style=flat)](https://github.com/Boilertalk/Web3.swift/stargazers) - Web3 library for interacting with the Ethereum blockchain.
- [web3swift](https://github.com/web3swift-team/web3swift) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/web3swift-team/web3swift?style=flat)](https://github.com/web3swift-team/web3swift/stargazers) - Elegant Web3js functionality in Swift. Native ABI parsing and smart contract interactions.

**[back to top](#contributing-and-collaborating)**

## Books

*Most recommended books*

- [Advanced Swift by Chris Eidhof, Ole Begemann, and Airspeed Velocity](https://www.objc.io/books/advanced-swift/)
- [Anyone Can Create an App by Wendy L. Wise](https://www.manning.com/books/anyone-can-create-an-app)
- [Classic Computer Science Problems in Swift](https://www.manning.com/books/classic-computer-science-problems-in-swift)
- [Cocoa Design Patterns](https://www.amazon.com/Cocoa-Design-Patterns-Erik-Buck/dp/0321535022)
- [Core Data by Florian Kugler and Daniel Eggert](https://www.objc.io/books/core-data/)
- [Functional Swift by Chris Eidhof, Florian Kugler, and Wouter Swierstra](https://www.objc.io/books/functional-swift/)
- [Hello Swift! by Tanmay Bakshi with Lynn Beighley](https://www.manning.com/books/hello-swift)
- [iOS Development with Swift by Craig Grummitt](https://www.manning.com/books/ios-development-with-swift)
- [iOS Programming: The Big Nerd Ranch Guide by Christian Keur, Aaron Hillegass](https://www.bignerdranch.com/books/ios-programming-the-big-nerd-ranch-guide-seventh-edition/)
- [Programming in Objective-C by Stephen G. Kochan](https://www.amazon.com/Programming-Objective-C-6th-Developers-Library/dp/0321967607)
- [Swift in Depth](https://www.manning.com/books/swift-in-depth)
- [The Complete Friday Q & A: Volume 1](https://www.mikeash.com/book.html)
- [The Swift Programming Language by Apple](https://books.apple.com/us/book/swift-programming-language/id881256329)

**[back to top](#contributing-and-collaborating)**

## Cache

*Thread safe, offline and high performance cache libs and frameworks.*

- [Awesome Cache](https://github.com/aschuch/AwesomeCache) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/aschuch/AwesomeCache?style=flat)](https://github.com/aschuch/AwesomeCache/stargazers) - Delightful on-disk cache (written in Swift).
- [Cache](https://github.com/hyperoslo/Cache) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/hyperoslo/Cache?style=flat)](https://github.com/hyperoslo/Cache/stargazers) - Nothing but Cache.
- [Disk](https://github.com/saoudrizwan/Disk) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/saoudrizwan/Disk?style=flat)](https://github.com/saoudrizwan/Disk/stargazers) - Delightful framework for iOS to easily persist structs, images, and data.
- [HanekeSwift](https://github.com/Haneke/HanekeSwift) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/Haneke/HanekeSwift?style=flat)](https://github.com/Haneke/HanekeSwift/stargazers) - A lightweight generic cache for iOS written in Swift with extra love for images.
- [mattress](https://github.com/buzzfeed/mattress) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/buzzfeed/mattress?style=flat)](https://github.com/buzzfeed/mattress/stargazers) - iOS Offline Caching for Web Content.
- [PINCache](https://github.com/pinterest/PINCache) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/pinterest/PINCache?style=flat)](https://github.com/pinterest/PINCache/stargazers) - Fast, non-deadlocking parallel object cache for iOS and macOS.
- [RocketData](https://github.com/plivesey/RocketData) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/plivesey/RocketData?style=flat)](https://github.com/plivesey/RocketData/stargazers) - A caching and consistency solution for immutable models.
- [SPTPersistentCache](https://github.com/spotify/SPTPersistentCache) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/spotify/SPTPersistentCache?style=flat)](https://github.com/spotify/SPTPersistentCache/stargazers) - Everyone tries to implement a cache at some point in their iOS app’s lifecycle, and this is ours. By Spotify.
- [Track](https://github.com/maquannene/Track) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/maquannene/Track?style=flat)](https://github.com/maquannene/Track/stargazers) - Track is a thread safe cache write by Swift. Composed of DiskCache and MemoryCache which support LRU.
- [YYCache](https://github.com/ibireme/YYCache) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/ibireme/YYCache?style=flat)](https://github.com/ibireme/YYCache/stargazers) - High performance cache framework for iOS.

**[back to top](#contributing-and-collaborating)**

## Code Quality

- [SwiftCop](https://github.com/andresinaka/SwiftCop) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/andresinaka/SwiftCop?style=flat)](https://github.com/andresinaka/SwiftCop/stargazers) -  SwiftCop is a validation library fully written in Swift and inspired by the clarity of Ruby On Rails Active Record validations.

- [AsyncNinja](https://github.com/AsyncNinja/AsyncNinja) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/AsyncNinja/AsyncNinja?style=flat)](https://github.com/AsyncNinja/AsyncNinja/stargazers) - A complete set of concurrency and reactive programming primitives.

- [PredicateFlow](https://github.com/andreadelfante/PredicateFlow) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/andreadelfante/PredicateFlow?style=flat)](https://github.com/andreadelfante/PredicateFlow/stargazers) - Write amazing, strong-typed and easy-to-read NSPredicate, allowing you to write flowable NSPredicate, without guessing attribution names, predicate operation or writing wrong arguments type.
- [PrediKit](https://github.com/KrakenDev/PrediKit) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/KrakenDev/PrediKit?style=flat)](https://github.com/KrakenDev/PrediKit/stargazers) - An NSPredicate DSL for iOS, macOS, tvOS, & watchOS. Inspired by SnapKit and lovingly written in Swift.
- [Skopelos](https://github.com/albertodebortoli/Skopelos) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/albertodebortoli/Skopelos?style=flat)](https://github.com/albertodebortoli/Skopelos/stargazers) - A minimalistic, thread safe, non-boilerplate and super easy to use version of Active Record on Core Data. ## Courses

*Online courses, tutorials and learning resources to kickstart your iOS development journey.*

### Getting Started

*Courses, tutorials, guides and bootcamps*

- [100 Days of SwiftUI](https://www.hackingwithswift.com/100/swiftui) - Free collection of videos and tutorials updated for iOS 15 and Swift 5.5.
- [Apple - Object-Oriented Programming with Objective-C](https://developer.apple.com/library/archive/documentation/Cocoa/Conceptual/OOP_ObjC/Introduction/Introduction.html)
- [ARStarter](https://github.com/codePrincess/ARStarter) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/codePrincess/ARStarter?style=flat)](https://github.com/codePrincess/ARStarter/stargazers) - Get started with ARKit - A little exercise for beginners.
- [Classpert - A list of 500 iOS Development courses (free and paid), from top e-learning platforms](https://classpert.com/ios-development) - Complete catalog of courses from Udacity, Pluralsight, Coursera, Edx, Treehouse and Skillshare.
- [iOS & Swift - The Complete iOS App Development Bootcamp](https://www.udemy.com/course/ios-13-app-development-bootcamp/)

## Database

*Wrappers, clients, Parse alternatives and safe tools to deal with ephemeral and persistent data.*

- [Couchbase Mobile](https://www.couchbase.com/products/mobile/) - Couchbase document store for mobile with cloud sync.
- [Default](https://github.com/Nirma/Default) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/Nirma/Default?style=flat)](https://github.com/Nirma/Default/stargazers) - Modern interface to UserDefaults + Codable support.
- [Defaults](https://github.com/sindresorhus/Defaults) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/sindresorhus/Defaults?style=flat)](https://github.com/sindresorhus/Defaults/stargazers) - Swifty and modern UserDefaults.
- [DuckDB](https://github.com/duckdb/duckdb-swift) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/duckdb/duckdb-swift?style=flat)](https://github.com/duckdb/duckdb-swift/stargazers) - DuckDB is a high-performance analytical database system.
- [FCModel](https://github.com/marcoarment/FCModel) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/marcoarment/FCModel?style=flat)](https://github.com/marcoarment/FCModel/stargazers) - An alternative to Core Data for people who like having direct SQL access.
- [Fluent](https://github.com/vapor/fluent) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/vapor/fluent?style=flat)](https://github.com/vapor/fluent/stargazers) - Simple ActiveRecord implementation for working with your database in Swift.
- [FMDB](https://github.com/ccgus/fmdb) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/ccgus/fmdb?style=flat)](https://github.com/ccgus/fmdb/stargazers) - A Cocoa / Objective-C wrapper around SQLite.
- [GRDB.swift](https://github.com/groue/GRDB.swift) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/groue/GRDB.swift?style=flat)](https://github.com/groue/GRDB.swift/stargazers) - A versatile SQLite toolkit for Swift, with WAL mode support.
- [IceCream](https://github.com/caiyue1993/IceCream) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/caiyue1993/IceCream?style=flat)](https://github.com/caiyue1993/IceCream/stargazers) - Sync Realm Database with CloudKit.
- [MMKV](https://github.com/Tencent/MMKV) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/Tencent/MMKV?style=flat)](https://github.com/Tencent/MMKV/stargazers) - An efficient, small mobile key-value storage framework developed by WeChat. Works on iOS, Android, macOS and Windows.
- [MongoKitten](https://github.com/OpenKitten/MongoKitten) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/OpenKitten/MongoKitten?style=flat)](https://github.com/OpenKitten/MongoKitten/stargazers) - A pure Swift MongoDB client implementation with support for embedded databases.
- [MySQL](https://github.com/PerfectlySoft/Perfect-MySQL) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/PerfectlySoft/Perfect-MySQL?style=flat)](https://github.com/PerfectlySoft/Perfect-MySQL/stargazers) - A Swift wrapper around the MySQL client library, enabling access to MySQL servers.
- [Nora](https://github.com/SD10/Nora) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/SD10/Nora?style=flat)](https://github.com/SD10/Nora/stargazers) - Nora is a Firebase abstraction layer for working with FirebaseDatabase and FirebaseStorage.
- [ObjectBox](https://github.com/objectbox/objectbox-swift) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/objectbox/objectbox-swift?style=flat)](https://github.com/objectbox/objectbox-swift/stargazers) - ObjectBox is a superfast, light-weight object persistence framework.
- [OHMySQL](https://github.com/oleghnidets/OHMySQL) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/oleghnidets/OHMySQL?style=flat)](https://github.com/oleghnidets/OHMySQL/stargazers) - An Objective-C wrapper of MySQL C API.
- [PersistenceKit](https://github.com/Teknasyon-Teknoloji/PersistenceKit) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/Teknasyon-Teknoloji/PersistenceKit?style=flat)](https://github.com/Teknasyon-Teknoloji/PersistenceKit/stargazers) - Store and retrieve Codable objects to various persistence layers, in a couple lines of code.
- [PersistentStorageSerializable](https://github.com/IvanRublev/PersistentStorageSerializable) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/IvanRublev/PersistentStorageSerializable?style=flat)](https://github.com/IvanRublev/PersistentStorageSerializable/stargazers) - Swift library that makes easier to serialize the user's preferences (app's settings) with system User Defaults or Property List file on disk.
- [Prephirences](https://github.com/phimage/Prephirences) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/phimage/Prephirences?style=flat)](https://github.com/phimage/Prephirences/stargazers) - Prephirences is a Swift library that provides useful protocols and convenience methods to manage application preferences, configurations and app-state.
- [Realm](https://github.com/realm/realm-cocoa) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/realm/realm-cocoa?style=flat)](https://github.com/realm/realm-cocoa/stargazers) - The alternative to CoreData and SQLite: Simple, modern and fast.
- [RealmGeoQueries](https://github.com/mhergon/RealmGeoQueries) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/mhergon/RealmGeoQueries?style=flat)](https://github.com/mhergon/RealmGeoQueries/stargazers) - RealmGeoQueries simplifies spatial queries with Realm Cocoa. In the absence of and official functions, this library provide the possibility to do proximity search.
- [SecureDefaults](https://github.com/vpeschenkov/SecureDefaults) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/vpeschenkov/SecureDefaults?style=flat)](https://github.com/vpeschenkov/SecureDefaults/stargazers) - A lightweight wrapper over UserDefaults/NSUserDefaults with an extra AES-256 encryption layer.
- [Shallows](https://github.com/dreymonde/Shallows) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/dreymonde/Shallows?style=flat)](https://github.com/dreymonde/Shallows/stargazers) - Your lightweight persistence toolbox.
- [SQLite.swift](https://github.com/stephencelis/SQLite.swift) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/stephencelis/SQLite.swift?style=flat)](https://github.com/stephencelis/SQLite.swift/stargazers) - A type-safe, Swift-language layer over SQLite3.
- [StorageKit](https://github.com/StorageKit/StorageKit) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/StorageKit/StorageKit?style=flat)](https://github.com/StorageKit/StorageKit/stargazers) - Your Data Storage Troubleshooter.
- [SugarRecord](https://github.com/modo-studio/SugarRecord) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/modo-studio/SugarRecord?style=flat)](https://github.com/modo-studio/SugarRecord/stargazers)  - Data persistence management library.
- [SwiftStore](https://github.com/hemantasapkota/SwiftStore) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/hemantasapkota/SwiftStore?style=flat)](https://github.com/hemantasapkota/SwiftStore/stargazers) - Key-Value store for Swift backed by LevelDB.
- [SwiftyUserDefaults](https://github.com/sunshinejr/SwiftyUserDefaults) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/sunshinejr/SwiftyUserDefaults?style=flat)](https://github.com/sunshinejr/SwiftyUserDefaults/stargazers) - Statically-typed NSUserDefaults.
- [TypedDefaults](https://github.com/tasanobu/TypedDefaults) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/tasanobu/TypedDefaults?style=flat)](https://github.com/tasanobu/TypedDefaults/stargazers) - TypedDefaults is a utility library to type-safely use NSUserDefaults.
- [Unrealm](https://github.com/arturdev/Unrealm) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/arturdev/Unrealm?style=flat)](https://github.com/arturdev/Unrealm/stargazers) - Unrealm enables you to easily store Swift native Classes, Structs and Enums into Realm.

- [WCDB](https://github.com/Tencent/wcdb) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/Tencent/wcdb?style=flat)](https://github.com/Tencent/wcdb/stargazers) - WCDB is an efficient, complete, easy-to-use mobile database framework for iOS, macOS.

## Data Structures / Algorithms

*Diffs, keypaths, sorted lists and other amazing data structures wrappers and libraries.*

- [Algorithm](https://github.com/CosmicMind/Algorithm) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/CosmicMind/Algorithm?style=flat)](https://github.com/CosmicMind/Algorithm/stargazers) - Algorithm is a collection of data structures that are empowered by a probability toolset.
- [BTree](https://github.com/attaswift/BTree) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/attaswift/BTree?style=flat)](https://github.com/attaswift/BTree/stargazers) - Fast ordered collections for Swift using in-memory B-trees.
- [Buffer](https://github.com/alexdrone/Buffer) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/alexdrone/Buffer?style=flat)](https://github.com/alexdrone/Buffer/stargazers) - Swift μ-framework for efficient array diffs, collection observation and cell configuration.
- [Changeset](https://github.com/osteslag/Changeset) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/osteslag/Changeset?style=flat)](https://github.com/osteslag/Changeset/stargazers) - Minimal edits from one collection to another.
- [Differ](https://github.com/tonyarnold/Differ) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/tonyarnold/Differ?style=flat)](https://github.com/tonyarnold/Differ/stargazers) - Swift library to generate differences and patches between collections.
- [DifferenceKit](https://github.com/ra1028/DifferenceKit) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/ra1028/DifferenceKit?style=flat)](https://github.com/ra1028/DifferenceKit/stargazers) - A fast and flexible O(n) difference algorithm framework for Swift collection.
- [Differific](https://github.com/zenangst/Differific) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/zenangst/Differific?style=flat)](https://github.com/zenangst/Differific/stargazers) - A fast and convenient diffing framework.
- [Dispatch](https://github.com/alexdrone/Store) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/alexdrone/Store?style=flat)](https://github.com/alexdrone/Store/stargazers) - Multi-store Flux implementation in Swift.
- [Dollar](https://github.com/ankurp/Dollar) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/ankurp/Dollar?style=flat)](https://github.com/ankurp/Dollar/stargazers) - A functional tool-belt for Swift Language similar to Lo-Dash or Underscore.js in Javascript https://www.dollarswift.org/.
- [EKAlgorithms](https://github.com/EvgenyKarkan/EKAlgorithms) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/EvgenyKarkan/EKAlgorithms?style=flat)](https://github.com/EvgenyKarkan/EKAlgorithms/stargazers) - Some well known CS algorithms & data structures in Objective-C.
- [HeckelDiff](https://github.com/mcudich/HeckelDiff) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/mcudich/HeckelDiff?style=flat)](https://github.com/mcudich/HeckelDiff/stargazers) - A fast Swift diffing library.
- [KeyPathKit](https://github.com/vincent-pradeilles/KeyPathKit) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/vincent-pradeilles/KeyPathKit?style=flat)](https://github.com/vincent-pradeilles/KeyPathKit/stargazers) - KeyPathKit provides a seamless syntax to manipulate data using typed keypaths.
- [Result](https://github.com/antitypical/Result) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/antitypical/Result?style=flat)](https://github.com/antitypical/Result/stargazers) - Swift type modeling the success/failure of arbitrary operations.
- [swift-algorithm-club](https://github.com/raywenderlich/swift-algorithm-club) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/raywenderlich/swift-algorithm-club?style=flat)](https://github.com/raywenderlich/swift-algorithm-club/stargazers) - Algorithms and data structures in Swift, with explanations!
- [SwiftGraph](https://github.com/davecom/SwiftGraph) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/davecom/SwiftGraph?style=flat)](https://github.com/davecom/SwiftGraph/stargazers) - Graph data structure and utility functions in pure Swift.
- [SwiftPriorityQueue](https://github.com/davecom/SwiftPriorityQueue) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/davecom/SwiftPriorityQueue?style=flat)](https://github.com/davecom/SwiftPriorityQueue/stargazers) - A priority queue with a classic binary heap implementation in pure Swift.

## Debugging

*Debugging tools, crash reports, logs and console UI's.*

- [AEConsole](https://github.com/tadija/AEConsole) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/tadija/AEConsole?style=flat)](https://github.com/tadija/AEConsole/stargazers) - Customizable Console UI overlay with debug log on top of your iOS App.
- [Alpha](https://github.com/Legoless/Alpha) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/Legoless/Alpha?style=flat)](https://github.com/Legoless/Alpha/stargazers) - Next generation debugging framework for iOS.
- [AppSpector](https://appspector.com) - Remote iOS and Android debugging and data collection service. You can debug networking, logs, CoreData, SQLite, NSNotificationCenter and mock device's geo location.
- [Atlantis](https://github.com/ProxymanApp/atlantis) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/ProxymanApp/atlantis?style=flat)](https://github.com/ProxymanApp/atlantis/stargazers) - A little and powerful iOS framework for intercepting HTTP/HTTPS Traffic from your iOS app. No more messing around with proxy and certificate config. Inspect Traffic Log with Proxyman app.
- [chisel](https://github.com/facebook/chisel) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/facebook/chisel?style=flat)](https://github.com/facebook/chisel/stargazers) - Collection of LLDB commands to assist debugging iOS apps.
- [DBDebugToolkit](https://github.com/dbukowski/DBDebugToolkit) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/dbukowski/DBDebugToolkit?style=flat)](https://github.com/dbukowski/DBDebugToolkit/stargazers) - Set of easy to use debugging tools for iOS developers & QA engineers.
- [DebugSwift](https://github.com/DebugSwift/DebugSwift) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/DebugSwift/DebugSwift?style=flat)](https://github.com/DebugSwift/DebugSwift/stargazers) - A comprehensive toolkit designed to simplify and enhance the debugging process for iOS applications.
- [DoraemonKit](https://github.com/didi/DoraemonKit) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/didi/DoraemonKit?style=flat)](https://github.com/didi/DoraemonKit/stargazers) - A full-featured iOS App development assistant，30+ tools included. You deserve it.
- [Flex](https://github.com/Flipboard/FLEX) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/Flipboard/FLEX?style=flat)](https://github.com/Flipboard/FLEX/stargazers) - An in-app debugging and exploration tool for iOS.
- [Httper-iOS](https://github.com/MuShare/Httper-iOS) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/MuShare/Httper-iOS?style=flat)](https://github.com/MuShare/Httper-iOS/stargazers) - App for developers to test REST API.
- [Hyperion](https://github.com/willowtreeapps/Hyperion-iOS) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/willowtreeapps/Hyperion-iOS?style=flat)](https://github.com/willowtreeapps/Hyperion-iOS/stargazers) - In-app design review tool to inspect measurements, attributes, and animations.
- [LayoutInspector](https://github.com/isavynskyi/LayoutInspector) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/isavynskyi/LayoutInspector?style=flat)](https://github.com/isavynskyi/LayoutInspector/stargazers) - Debug app layouts directly on iOS device: inspect layers in 3D and debug each visible view attributes.
- [MTHawkeye](https://github.com/meitu/MTHawkeye) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/meitu/MTHawkeye?style=flat)](https://github.com/meitu/MTHawkeye/stargazers) - Profiling / Debugging assist tools for iOS, include tools: UITimeProfiler, Memory Allocations, Living ObjC Objects Sniffer, Network Transaction Waterfall, etc.
- [Netfox](https://github.com/kasketis/netfox) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/kasketis/netfox?style=flat)](https://github.com/kasketis/netfox/stargazers) - A lightweight, one line setup, iOS / macOS network debugging library!
- [NetworkEye](https://github.com/coderyi/NetworkEye) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/coderyi/NetworkEye?style=flat)](https://github.com/coderyi/NetworkEye/stargazers) - a iOS network debug library, It can monitor HTTP requests within the App and displays information related to the request.
- [Playbook](https://github.com/playbook-ui/playbook-ios) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/playbook-ui/playbook-ios?style=flat)](https://github.com/playbook-ui/playbook-ios/stargazers) - A library for isolated developing UI components and automatically snapshots of them.
- [PonyDebugger](https://github.com/square/PonyDebugger) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/square/PonyDebugger?style=flat)](https://github.com/square/PonyDebugger/stargazers) - Remote network and data debugging for your native iOS app using Chrome Developer Tools.
- [Scyther](https://github.com/bstillitano/Scyther) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/bstillitano/Scyther?style=flat)](https://github.com/bstillitano/Scyther/stargazers) - A full-featured, in-app debugging menu packed full of useful tools including network logging, layout inspection, location spoofing, console logging and so much more.
- [Woodpecker](http://www.woodpeck.cn) - View sandbox files, UserDefaults, network request from Mac.
- [Wormholy](https://github.com/pmusolino/Wormholy) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/pmusolino/Wormholy?style=flat)](https://github.com/pmusolino/Wormholy/stargazers) - iOS network debugging, like a wizard.
- [Xniffer](https://github.com/xmartlabs/Xniffer) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/xmartlabs/Xniffer?style=flat)](https://github.com/xmartlabs/Xniffer/stargazers) - A swift network profiler built on top of URLSession.

## Dependency Injection

*Dependency injection frameworks and libraries for decoupled, testable iOS code.*

- [DITranquillity](https://github.com/ivlevAstef/DITranquillity) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/ivlevAstef/DITranquillity?style=flat)](https://github.com/ivlevAstef/DITranquillity/stargazers) - Dependency injection framework for iOS applications written in clean Swift.
- [Needle](https://github.com/uber/needle) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/uber/needle?style=flat)](https://github.com/uber/needle/stargazers) — Compile-time safe Swift dependency injection framework with real code.
- [Perform](https://github.com/thoughtbot/Perform) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/thoughtbot/Perform?style=flat)](https://github.com/thoughtbot/Perform/stargazers) - Easy dependency injection for storyboard segues.
- [SafeDI](https://github.com/dfed/safedi) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/dfed/safedi?style=flat)](https://github.com/dfed/safedi/stargazers) - Compile-time safe dependency injection in Swift 6.
- [Swinject](https://github.com/Swinject/Swinject) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/Swinject/Swinject?style=flat)](https://github.com/Swinject/Swinject/stargazers) - Dependency injection framework for Swift.

## Dependency / Package Manager

*Tools to manage third-party dependencies and packages in your iOS projects.*

- [Accio](https://github.com/JamitLabs/Accio) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/JamitLabs/Accio?style=flat)](https://github.com/JamitLabs/Accio/stargazers) - A SwiftPM based dependency manager for iOS & Co. with improvements over Carthage.
- [Carthage](https://github.com/Carthage/Carthage) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/Carthage/Carthage?style=flat)](https://github.com/Carthage/Carthage/stargazers) - A simple, decentralized dependency manager for Cocoa.
- [CocoaPods](https://cocoapods.org/) - CocoaPods is the dependency manager for Objective-C projects. It has thousands of libraries and can help you scale your projects elegantly.
- [Rome](https://github.com/tmspzz/Rome) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/tmspzz/Rome?style=flat)](https://github.com/tmspzz/Rome/stargazers) - A cache tool for Carthage built frameworks.
- [swift-package-manager](https://github.com/apple/swift-package-manager) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/apple/swift-package-manager?style=flat)](https://github.com/apple/swift-package-manager/stargazers) - The Package Manager for the Swift Programming Language.
- [Xcode Maven](http://sap-production.github.io/xcode-maven-plugin/site/) - The Xcode Maven Plugin can be used in order to run Xcode builds embedded in a Maven lifecycle.

## Deployment / Distribution

*Continuous integration, delivery and distribution tools for shipping iOS apps.*

- [AppCenter](https://appcenter.ms) - Continuously build, test, release, and monitor apps for every platform.
- [Appcircle.io](https://appcircle.io) — An enterprise-grade mobile DevOps platform that automates the build, test, and publish store of mobile apps for faster, efficient release cycle
- [AppLaunchpad](https://theapplaunchpad.com/) - Free App Store screenshot builder.
- [Bitrise](https://www.bitrise.io) - Mobile Continuous Integration & Delivery with dozens of integrations to build, test, deploy and collaborate.
- [boarding](https://github.com/fastlane/boarding) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/fastlane/boarding?style=flat)](https://github.com/fastlane/boarding/stargazers) - Instantly create a simple signup page for TestFlight beta testers.
- [buddybuild](https://www.buddybuild.com/) - A mobile iteration platform - build, deploy, and collaborate.
- [Codemagic](https://codemagic.io) - Build, test and deliver iOS apps 20% faster with Codemagic CI/CD.
- [Crashlytics](https://firebase.google.com/products/crashlytics/) - A crash reporting and beta testing service.
- [deliver](https://github.com/fastlane/fastlane/tree/master/deliver) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/fastlane/fastlane/tree/master/deliver?style=flat)](https://github.com/fastlane/fastlane/tree/master/deliver/stargazers) - Upload screenshots, metadata and your app to the App Store using a single command.
- [fastlane](https://github.com/fastlane/fastlane) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/fastlane/fastlane?style=flat)](https://github.com/fastlane/fastlane/stargazers) - Connect all iOS deployment tools into one streamlined workflow.
- [Instabug](https://instabug.com) - In-app feedback, Bug and Crash reporting, Fix Bugs Faster through user-steps, video recordings, screen annotation, network requests logging.
- [LaunchKit](https://github.com/LaunchKit/LaunchKit) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/LaunchKit/LaunchKit?style=flat)](https://github.com/LaunchKit/LaunchKit/stargazers) - A set of web-based tools for mobile app developers, now open source!
- [Rollout.io](https://rollout.io/) - SDK to patch, fix bugs, modify and manipulate native apps (Obj-c & Swift) in real-time.
- [Runway](https://runway.team) - Easier mobile releases for teams. Integrates across tools (version control, project management, CI, app stores, crash reporting, etc.) to provide a single source of truth for mobile teams to come together around during release cycles. Equal parts automation and collaboration.
- [Screenplay](https://screenplay.dev) - Instant rollbacks and canary deployments for iOS.
- [ScreenshotFramer](https://github.com/IdeasOnCanvas/ScreenshotFramer) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/IdeasOnCanvas/ScreenshotFramer?style=flat)](https://github.com/IdeasOnCanvas/ScreenshotFramer/stargazers) - With Screenshot Framer you can easily create nice-looking and localized App Store Images.
- [Semaphore](https://semaphoreci.com/product/ios) - CI/CD service which makes it easy to build, test and deploy applications for any Apple device. iOS support is fully integrated in Semaphore 2.0, so you can use the same powerful CI/CD pipeline features for iOS as you do for Linux-based development.
- [snapshot](https://github.com/fastlane/fastlane/tree/master/snapshot) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/fastlane/fastlane/tree/master/snapshot?style=flat)](https://github.com/fastlane/fastlane/tree/master/snapshot/stargazers) - Automate taking localized screenshots of your iOS app on every device.
- [TestFlight Beta Testing](https://developer.apple.com/testflight/) - The beta testing service hosted on iTunes Connect (requires iOS 8 or later).
- [watchbuild](https://github.com/fastlane/watchbuild) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/fastlane/watchbuild?style=flat)](https://github.com/fastlane/watchbuild/stargazers) - Get a notification once your iTunes Connect build is finished processing.

- [Bluetonium](https://github.com/e-sites/Bluetonium) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/e-sites/Bluetonium?style=flat)](https://github.com/e-sites/Bluetonium/stargazers) - Bluetooth mapping in Swift.
- [BluetoothKit](https://github.com/rhummelmose/BluetoothKit) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/rhummelmose/BluetoothKit?style=flat)](https://github.com/rhummelmose/BluetoothKit/stargazers) - Easily communicate between iOS/macOS devices using BLE.
- [Discovery](https://github.com/omergul/Discovery) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/omergul/Discovery?style=flat)](https://github.com/omergul/Discovery/stargazers) - A very simple library to discover and retrieve data from nearby devices (even if the peer app works at background).
- [LGBluetooth](https://github.com/LGBluetooth/LGBluetooth) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/LGBluetooth/LGBluetooth?style=flat)](https://github.com/LGBluetooth/LGBluetooth/stargazers) - Simple, block-based, lightweight library over CoreBluetooth. Will clean up your Core Bluetooth related code.
- [MultiPeer](https://github.com/dingwilson/MultiPeer) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/dingwilson/MultiPeer?style=flat)](https://github.com/dingwilson/MultiPeer/stargazers) - Multipeer is a wrapper for Apple's MultipeerConnectivity framework for offline data transmission between Apple devices. It makes easy to automatically connect to multiple nearby devices and share information using either bluetooth or wifi.
- [PeerKit](https://github.com/jpsim/PeerKit) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/jpsim/PeerKit?style=flat)](https://github.com/jpsim/PeerKit/stargazers) An open-source Swift framework for building event-driven, zero-config Multipeer Connectivity apps.

**[back to top](#contributing-and-collaborating)**

CoreMotion now made insanely simple.

## Layout

*Auto Layout, UI frameworks and a gorgeous list of tools to simplify layout constructions*

- [Anchorage](https://github.com/Rightpoint/Anchorage) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/Rightpoint/Anchorage?style=flat)](https://github.com/Rightpoint/Anchorage/stargazers) - A collection of operators and utilities that simplify iOS layout code.
- [Auto Layout Magic](http://akordadev.github.io/AutoLayoutMagic/) - Build 1 scene, let Auto Layout Magic generate the  constraints for you!  Scenes look great across all devices!
- [BrickKit](https://github.com/wayfair/brickkit-ios) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/wayfair/brickkit-ios?style=flat)](https://github.com/wayfair/brickkit-ios/stargazers) - With BrickKit, you can create complex and responsive layouts in a simple way. It's easy to use and easy to extend. Create your own reusable bricks and behaviors.
- [Cartography](https://github.com/robb/Cartography) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/robb/Cartography?style=flat)](https://github.com/robb/Cartography/stargazers) - A declarative Auto Layout DSL for Swift.
- [Cupcake](https://github.com/nerdycat/Cupcake) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/nerdycat/Cupcake?style=flat)](https://github.com/nerdycat/Cupcake/stargazers) - An easy way to create and layout UI components for iOS.
- [EasyPeasy](https://github.com/nakiostudio/EasyPeasy) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/nakiostudio/EasyPeasy?style=flat)](https://github.com/nakiostudio/EasyPeasy/stargazers) - Auto Layout made easy.
- [Façade](https://github.com/mamaral/Facade) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/mamaral/Facade?style=flat)](https://github.com/mamaral/Facade/stargazers) - Programmatic view layout for the rest of us - an autolayout alternative.
- [FDTemplateLayoutCell](https://github.com/forkingdog/UITableView-FDTemplateLayoutCell) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/forkingdog/UITableView-FDTemplateLayoutCell?style=flat)](https://github.com/forkingdog/UITableView-FDTemplateLayoutCell/stargazers) - Template auto layout cell for automatically UITableViewCell height calculating.
- [FlexLayout](https://github.com/layoutBox/FlexLayout) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/layoutBox/FlexLayout?style=flat)](https://github.com/layoutBox/FlexLayout/stargazers) - FlexLayout gently wraps the highly optimized [facebook/yoga](https://github.com/facebook/yoga) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/facebook/yoga?style=flat)](https://github.com/facebook/yoga/stargazers) flexbox implementation in a concise, intuitive & chainable syntax.
- [FLKAutoLayout](https://github.com/floriankugler/FLKAutoLayout) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/floriankugler/FLKAutoLayout?style=flat)](https://github.com/floriankugler/FLKAutoLayout/stargazers) - UIView category which makes it easy to create layout constraints in code.
- [Grid](https://github.com/exyte/Grid) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/exyte/Grid?style=flat)](https://github.com/exyte/Grid/stargazers) - The most powerful Grid container missed in SwiftUI.
- [Layout](https://github.com/nicklockwood/layout) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/nicklockwood/layout?style=flat)](https://github.com/nicklockwood/layout/stargazers) - A declarative UI framework for iOS.
- [Layoutless](https://github.com/DeclarativeHub/Layoutless) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/DeclarativeHub/Layoutless?style=flat)](https://github.com/DeclarativeHub/Layoutless/stargazers) - Minimalistic declarative layout and styling framework built on top of Auto Layout.
- [ManualLayout](https://github.com/isair/ManualLayout) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/isair/ManualLayout?style=flat)](https://github.com/isair/ManualLayout/stargazers) - Easy to use and flexible library for manually laying out views and layers for iOS and tvOS. Supports AsyncDisplayKit.
- [Masonry](https://github.com/SnapKit/Masonry) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/SnapKit/Masonry?style=flat)](https://github.com/SnapKit/Masonry/stargazers) - Harness the power of AutoLayout NSLayoutConstraints with a simplified, chainable and expressive syntax.
- [MisterFusion](https://github.com/marty-suzuki/MisterFusion) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/marty-suzuki/MisterFusion?style=flat)](https://github.com/marty-suzuki/MisterFusion/stargazers) - A Swift DSL for AutoLayout. It is the extremely clear, but concise syntax, in addition, can be used in both Swift and Objective-C.
- [MondrianLayout](https://github.com/muukii/MondrianLayout) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/muukii/MondrianLayout?style=flat)](https://github.com/muukii/MondrianLayout/stargazers) - A DSL based layout builder for AutoLayout.
- [MyLinearLayout](https://github.com/youngsoft/MyLinearLayout) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/youngsoft/MyLinearLayout?style=flat)](https://github.com/youngsoft/MyLinearLayout/stargazers) - MyLayout is a powerful iOS UI framework implemented by Objective-C. It integrates the functions with Android Layout,iOS AutoLayout,SizeClass, HTML CSS float and flexbox and bootstrap.
- [Neon](https://github.com/mamaral/Neon) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/mamaral/Neon?style=flat)](https://github.com/mamaral/Neon/stargazers) - A powerful Swift programmatic UI layout framework.
- [PinLayout](https://github.com/layoutBox/PinLayout) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/layoutBox/PinLayout?style=flat)](https://github.com/layoutBox/PinLayout/stargazers) - Fast Swift Views layouting without auto layout. No magic, pure code, full control and blazing fast. Concise syntax, intuitive, readable & chainable.
- [PureLayout](https://github.com/PureLayout/PureLayout) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/PureLayout/PureLayout?style=flat)](https://github.com/PureLayout/PureLayout/stargazers) - The ultimate API for iOS & macOS Auto Layout — impressively simple, immensely powerful. Objective-C and Swift compatible.
- [QuickLayout](https://github.com/huri000/QuickLayout) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/huri000/QuickLayout?style=flat)](https://github.com/huri000/QuickLayout/stargazers) - QuickLayout offers a simple way, to easily manage Auto Layout in code.
- [Relayout](https://github.com/stevestreza/Relayout) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/stevestreza/Relayout?style=flat)](https://github.com/stevestreza/Relayout/stargazers) - Swift microframework for declaring Auto Layout constraints functionally.
- [SnapKit](https://github.com/SnapKit/SnapKit) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/SnapKit/SnapKit?style=flat)](https://github.com/SnapKit/SnapKit/stargazers) - A Swift Autolayout DSL for iOS & macOS.
- [Stevia](https://github.com/freshOS/Stevia) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/freshOS/Stevia?style=flat)](https://github.com/freshOS/Stevia/stargazers) - Elegant view layout for iOS.
- [SwiftAutoLayout](https://github.com/indragiek/SwiftAutoLayout) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/indragiek/SwiftAutoLayout?style=flat)](https://github.com/indragiek/SwiftAutoLayout/stargazers) - Tiny Swift DSL for Autolayout.
- [SwiftBond](https://github.com/DeclarativeHub/Bond) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/DeclarativeHub/Bond?style=flat)](https://github.com/DeclarativeHub/Bond/stargazers) - Bond is a Swift binding framework that takes binding concepts to a whole new level. It's simple, powerful, type-safe and multi-paradigm.
- [SwiftBox](https://github.com/joshaber/SwiftBox) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/joshaber/SwiftBox?style=flat)](https://github.com/joshaber/SwiftBox/stargazers) - Flexbox in Swift, using Facebook's css-layout.
- [Swiftstraints](https://github.com/Skyvive/Swiftstraints) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/Skyvive/Swiftstraints?style=flat)](https://github.com/Skyvive/Swiftstraints/stargazers) - Auto Layout In Swift Made Easy.
- [TinyConstraints](https://github.com/roberthein/TinyConstraints) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/roberthein/TinyConstraints?style=flat)](https://github.com/roberthein/TinyConstraints/stargazers) -  The syntactic sugar that makes Auto Layout sweeter for human use.
- [Yalta](https://github.com/kean/Align) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/kean/Align?style=flat)](https://github.com/kean/Align/stargazers) - An intuitive and powerful Auto Layout library.
- [YogaKit](https://github.com/facebook/yoga/tree/master/YogaKit) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/facebook/yoga/tree/master/YogaKit?style=flat)](https://github.com/facebook/yoga/tree/master/YogaKit/stargazers) - Powerful layout engine which implements Flexbox.

## Localization

*Tools to manage strings files, translate and enable localization in your apps.*

- [attranslate](https://github.com/fkirc/attranslate) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/fkirc/attranslate?style=flat)](https://github.com/fkirc/attranslate/stargazers) - Semi-automatically translate or synchronize .strings files or crossplatform-files from different languages.
- [BartyCrouch](https://github.com/Flinesoft/BartyCrouch) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/Flinesoft/BartyCrouch?style=flat)](https://github.com/Flinesoft/BartyCrouch/stargazers) - Incrementally update/translate your Strings files from Code and Storyboards/XIBs.
- [CrowdinSDK](https://github.com/crowdin/mobile-sdk-ios) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/crowdin/mobile-sdk-ios?style=flat)](https://github.com/crowdin/mobile-sdk-ios/stargazers) - Crowdin iOS SDK delivers all new translations from Crowdin project to the application immediately.
- [Hodor](https://github.com/Aufree/Hodor) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/Aufree/Hodor?style=flat)](https://github.com/Aufree/Hodor/stargazers) - Simple solution to localize your iOS App.
- [IBLocalizable](https://github.com/PiXeL16/IBLocalizable) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/PiXeL16/IBLocalizable?style=flat)](https://github.com/PiXeL16/IBLocalizable/stargazers) - Localize your views directly in Interface Builder with IBLocalizable.
- [L10n-swift](https://github.com/Decybel07/L10n-swift) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/Decybel07/L10n-swift?style=flat)](https://github.com/Decybel07/L10n-swift/stargazers) - Localization of an application with ability to change language "on the fly" and support for plural forms in any language.
- [LocalizationKit](https://github.com/willpowell8/LocalizationKit_iOS) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/willpowell8/LocalizationKit_iOS?style=flat)](https://github.com/willpowell8/LocalizationKit_iOS/stargazers) - Localization management in realtime from a web portal. Easily manage your texts and translations without redeploy and resubmission.
- [Localize](https://github.com/andresilvagomez/Localize) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/andresilvagomez/Localize?style=flat)](https://github.com/andresilvagomez/Localize/stargazers) - Easy tool to localize apps using JSON or Strings and of course IBDesignables with extensions for UI components.
- [Localize-Swift](https://github.com/marmelroy/Localize-Swift) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/marmelroy/Localize-Swift?style=flat)](https://github.com/marmelroy/Localize-Swift/stargazers) - Swift 2.0 friendly localization and i18n with in-app language switching.
- [locheck](https://github.com/Asana/locheck) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/Asana/locheck?style=flat)](https://github.com/Asana/locheck/stargazers) - Validate .strings, .stringsdict, and strings.xml files for correctness to avoid crashes and bad translations.
- [Respresso Localization Converter](https://respresso.io/localization-converter) - Multiplatform localization converter for iOS (.strings + Objective-C getters), Android (strings.xml) and Web (.json).
- [Rubustrings](https://github.com/dcordero/Rubustrings) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/dcordero/Rubustrings?style=flat)](https://github.com/dcordero/Rubustrings/stargazers) - Check the format and consistency of Localizable.strings files.
- [StringSwitch](https://stringswitch.com) - Easily convert iOS .strings files to Android strings.xml format and vice versa.
- [Swifternalization](https://github.com/tomkowz/Swifternalization) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/tomkowz/Swifternalization?style=flat)](https://github.com/tomkowz/Swifternalization/stargazers) - Localize iOS apps in a smarter way using JSON files. Swift framework.

**[back to top](#contributing-and-collaborating)**

Print log without any format control symbol! Change debug habit thoroughly!

Allows you to log details to the console (and optionally a file), just like you would have with NSLog or println, but with additional information, such as the date, function name, filename and line number.

- [Airstream](https://github.com/qasim/Airstream) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/qasim/Airstream?style=flat)](https://github.com/qasim/Airstream/stargazers) - A framework for streaming audio between Apple devices using AirPlay.

- [LFLiveKit](https://github.com/LaiFengiOS/LFLiveKit) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/LaiFengiOS/LFLiveKit?style=flat)](https://github.com/LaiFengiOS/LFLiveKit/stargazers) - H264 and AAC Hard coding，support GPUImage Beauty， rtmp transmission，weak network lost frame，Dynamic switching rate.
- [StreamingKit](https://github.com/tumtumtum/StreamingKit) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/tumtumtum/StreamingKit?style=flat)](https://github.com/tumtumtum/StreamingKit/stargazers) - A fast and extensible gapless AudioPlayer/AudioStreamer for macOS and iOS.

- [AVAnimator](http://www.modejong.com/AVAnimator/) - An open source iOS native library that makes it easy to implement non-trivial video/audio enabled apps.
- [AVPlayerViewController-Subtitles](https://github.com/mhergon/AVPlayerViewController-Subtitles) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/mhergon/AVPlayerViewController-Subtitles?style=flat)](https://github.com/mhergon/AVPlayerViewController-Subtitles/stargazers) - AVPlayerViewController-Subtitles is a library to display subtitles on iOS. It's built as a Swift extension and it's very easy to integrate.

## Networking

*HTTP clients, socket libraries, reachability helpers and networking utilities.*

- [AFNetworking+RetryPolicy](https://github.com/kubatruhlar/AFNetworking-RetryPolicy) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/kubatruhlar/AFNetworking-RetryPolicy?style=flat)](https://github.com/kubatruhlar/AFNetworking-RetryPolicy/stargazers) - An objective-c category that adds the ability to set the retry logic for requests made with AFNetworking.
- [AFNetworking-Synchronous](https://github.com/paulmelnikow/AFNetworking-Synchronous) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/paulmelnikow/AFNetworking-Synchronous?style=flat)](https://github.com/paulmelnikow/AFNetworking-Synchronous/stargazers) - Synchronous requests for AFNetworking 1.x, 2.x, and 3.x.
- [Alamofire](https://github.com/Alamofire/Alamofire) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/Alamofire/Alamofire?style=flat)](https://github.com/Alamofire/Alamofire/stargazers) - Alamofire is an HTTP networking library written in Swift, from the creator of AFNetworking.
- [APIKit](https://github.com/ishkawa/APIKit) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/ishkawa/APIKit?style=flat)](https://github.com/ishkawa/APIKit/stargazers) - A networking library for building type safe web API client in Swift.
- [ASIHTTPRequest](https://github.com/pokeb/asi-http-request) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/pokeb/asi-http-request?style=flat)](https://github.com/pokeb/asi-http-request/stargazers) - Easy to use CFNetwork wrapper for HTTP requests, Objective-C, macOS and iPhone.
- [Bamboots](https://github.com/mmoaay/Bamboots) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/mmoaay/Bamboots?style=flat)](https://github.com/mmoaay/Bamboots/stargazers) - Bamboots is a network request framework based on Alamofire, aiming at making network request easier for business development.
- [CocoaAsyncSocket](https://github.com/robbiehanson/CocoaAsyncSocket) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/robbiehanson/CocoaAsyncSocket?style=flat)](https://github.com/robbiehanson/CocoaAsyncSocket/stargazers) - Asynchronous socket networking library for Mac and iOS.

- [FGRoute](https://github.com/Feghal/FGRoute) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/Feghal/FGRoute?style=flat)](https://github.com/Feghal/FGRoute/stargazers) - An easy-to-use library that helps developers to get wifi ssid, router and device ip addresses.

- [HappyDns](https://github.com/qiniu/happy-dns-objc) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/qiniu/happy-dns-objc?style=flat)](https://github.com/qiniu/happy-dns-objc/stargazers) - A Dns library, support custom dns server, dnspod httpdns. Only support A record.

## Notifications

*Local notifications, push services and notification UI tools.*

### Push Notifications

*Libraries and helpers for handling push notifications on iOS.*

- [Knuff](https://github.com/KnuffApp/Knuff) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/KnuffApp/Knuff?style=flat)](https://github.com/KnuffApp/Knuff/stargazers) - The debug application for Apple Push Notification Service (APNS).
- [NWPusher](https://github.com/noodlewerk/NWPusher) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/noodlewerk/NWPusher?style=flat)](https://github.com/noodlewerk/NWPusher/stargazers) - macOS and iOS application and framework to play with the Apple Push Notification service (APNs).
- [PEM](https://github.com/fastlane/fastlane/tree/master/pem) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/fastlane/fastlane/tree/master/pem?style=flat)](https://github.com/fastlane/fastlane/tree/master/pem/stargazers) - Automatically generate and renew your push notification profiles.
- [SimulatorRemoteNotifications](https://github.com/acoomans/SimulatorRemoteNotifications) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/acoomans/SimulatorRemoteNotifications?style=flat)](https://github.com/acoomans/SimulatorRemoteNotifications/stargazers) - Library to send mock remote notifications to the iOS simulator.

### Push Notification Providers

*Third-party services for sending push notifications to iOS devices.*

Most of these are paid services, some have free tiers.

- [Batch](https://batch.com)
- [Boxcar](https://boxcar.io)
- [Braze](https://www.braze.com/)
- [Carnival](https://www.sailthru.com)
- [Catapush](https://www.catapush.com/)
- [Growth Push](https://growthpush.com) - Popular in Japan.
- [Netmera](https://www.netmera.com/)
- [OneSignal](https://onesignal.com) - Free.
- [PushBots](https://pushbots.com/)
- [Pusher](https://pusher.com/beams) - Free and unlimited.
- [Pushkin](https://github.com/Nordeus/pushkin) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/Nordeus/pushkin?style=flat)](https://github.com/Nordeus/pushkin/stargazers) - Free and open-source.
- [Pushwoosh](https://www.pushwoosh.com)
- [Swrve](https://www.swrve.com)
- [Urban Airship](https://www.airship.com/platform/channels/mobile-app/)

## Objective-C Runtime

*Objective-C Runtime wrappers, libraries and tools.*

- [Lumos](https://github.com/sushinoya/lumos) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/sushinoya/lumos?style=flat)](https://github.com/sushinoya/lumos/stargazers) - A light Swift wrapper around Objective-C Runtime.
- [Swizzlean](https://github.com/rbaumbach/Swizzlean) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/rbaumbach/Swizzlean?style=flat)](https://github.com/rbaumbach/Swizzlean/stargazers) - An Objective-C Swizzle Helper Class.

## Parsing

*Parsers and serializers for common data formats.*

### CSV

*Libraries for reading and writing CSV files in Swift and Objective-C.*

- [CodableCSV](https://github.com/dehesa/CodableCSV) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/dehesa/CodableCSV?style=flat)](https://github.com/dehesa/CodableCSV/stargazers) - Read and write CSV files row-by-row & field-by-field or through Swift's Codable interface.
- [CSV.swift](https://github.com/yaslab/CSV.swift) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/yaslab/CSV.swift?style=flat)](https://github.com/yaslab/CSV.swift/stargazers) - CSV reading and writing library written in Swift.
- [CSwiftV](https://github.com/Daniel1of1/CSwiftV) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/Daniel1of1/CSwiftV?style=flat)](https://github.com/Daniel1of1/CSwiftV/stargazers) - A csv parser written in swift conforming to rfc4180.

**[back to top](#contributing-and-collaborating)**

### JSON

*JSON parsing, mapping and serialization libraries.*

- [AlamofireObjectMapper](https://github.com/tristanhimmelman/AlamofireObjectMapper) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/tristanhimmelman/AlamofireObjectMapper?style=flat)](https://github.com/tristanhimmelman/AlamofireObjectMapper/stargazers) - An Alamofire extension which converts JSON response data into swift objects using ObjectMapper.
- [Arrow 🏹](https://github.com/freshOS/Arrow) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/freshOS/Arrow?style=flat)](https://github.com/freshOS/Arrow/stargazers) - Elegant JSON Parsing in Swift.
- [Elevate](https://github.com/Nike-Inc/Elevate) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/Nike-Inc/Elevate?style=flat)](https://github.com/Nike-Inc/Elevate/stargazers) - Elevate is a JSON parsing framework that leverages Swift to make parsing simple, reliable and composable.
- [FastEasyMapping](https://github.com/Yalantis/FastEasyMapping) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/Yalantis/FastEasyMapping?style=flat)](https://github.com/Yalantis/FastEasyMapping/stargazers) - Serialize & deserialize JSON fast.
- [FlatBuffersSwift](https://github.com/mzaks/FlatBuffersSwift) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/mzaks/FlatBuffersSwift?style=flat)](https://github.com/mzaks/FlatBuffersSwift/stargazers) - This project brings FlatBuffers (an efficient cross platform serialization library) to Swift.
- [Groot](https://github.com/gonzalezreal/Groot) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/gonzalezreal/Groot?style=flat)](https://github.com/gonzalezreal/Groot/stargazers) - Convert JSON dictionaries and arrays to and from Core Data managed objects.
- [HandyJSON](https://github.com/alibaba/handyjson) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/alibaba/handyjson?style=flat)](https://github.com/alibaba/handyjson/stargazers) - A handy swift JSON-object serialization/deserialization library for Swift.
- [Himotoki](https://github.com/ikesyo/Himotoki) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/ikesyo/Himotoki?style=flat)](https://github.com/ikesyo/Himotoki/stargazers) - A type-safe JSON decoding library purely written in Swift.
- [JASON](https://github.com/delba/JASON) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/delba/JASON?style=flat)](https://github.com/delba/JASON/stargazers) - JSON parsing with outstanding performances and convenient operators.
- [JAYSON](https://github.com/muukii/JAYSON) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/muukii/JAYSON?style=flat)](https://github.com/muukii/JAYSON/stargazers) - Strict and Scalable JSON library.
- [jsoncafe.com](http://www.jsoncafe.com/) - Online Template driven Model Class Generator from JSON.
- [JSONExport](https://github.com/Ahmed-Ali/JSONExport) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/Ahmed-Ali/JSONExport?style=flat)](https://github.com/Ahmed-Ali/JSONExport/stargazers) - JSONExport is a desktop application for macOS which enables you to export JSON objects as model classes with their associated constructors, utility methods, setters and getters in your favorite language.
- [JSONModel](https://github.com/JSONModel/JSONModel) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/JSONModel/JSONModel?style=flat)](https://github.com/JSONModel/JSONModel/stargazers) - Magical Data Modeling Framework for JSON. Create rapidly powerful, atomic and smart data model classes.
- [Mantle](https://github.com/Mantle/Mantle) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/Mantle/Mantle?style=flat)](https://github.com/Mantle/Mantle/stargazers) - Model framework for Cocoa and Cocoa Touch.
- [Marshal](https://github.com/utahiosmac/Marshal) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/utahiosmac/Marshal?style=flat)](https://github.com/utahiosmac/Marshal/stargazers) - Marshaling the typeless wild west of [String: Any] (Protocol based).
- [MJExtension](https://github.com/CoderMJLee/MJExtension) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/CoderMJLee/MJExtension?style=flat)](https://github.com/CoderMJLee/MJExtension/stargazers) - A fast, convenient and nonintrusive conversion between JSON and model. Your model class don't need to extend another base class. You don't need to modify any model file.
- [ObjectMapper](https://github.com/tristanhimmelman/ObjectMapper) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/tristanhimmelman/ObjectMapper?style=flat)](https://github.com/tristanhimmelman/ObjectMapper/stargazers) - A framework written in Swift that makes it easy for you to convert your Model objects (Classes and Structs) to and from JSON.
- [PMHTTP](https://github.com/postmates/PMHTTP) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/postmates/PMHTTP?style=flat)](https://github.com/postmates/PMHTTP/stargazers) - Swift/Obj-C HTTP framework with a focus on REST and JSON.
- [PMJSON](https://github.com/postmates/PMJSON) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/postmates/PMJSON?style=flat)](https://github.com/postmates/PMJSON/stargazers) - Pure Swift JSON encoding/decoding library.
- [PropertyMapper](https://github.com/krzysztofzablocki/PropertyMapper) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/krzysztofzablocki/PropertyMapper?style=flat)](https://github.com/krzysztofzablocki/PropertyMapper/stargazers) - Data mapping and validation with minimal amount of code.
- [SBJson](https://github.com/SBJson/SBJson) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/SBJson/SBJson?style=flat)](https://github.com/SBJson/SBJson/stargazers) - This framework implements a strict JSON parser and generator in Objective-C.
- [SwiftyJSON](https://github.com/SwiftyJSON/SwiftyJSON) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/SwiftyJSON/SwiftyJSON?style=flat)](https://github.com/SwiftyJSON/SwiftyJSON/stargazers) - The better way to deal with JSON data in Swift.
- [SwiftyJSONAccelerator](https://github.com/insanoid/SwiftyJSONAccelerator) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/insanoid/SwiftyJSONAccelerator?style=flat)](https://github.com/insanoid/SwiftyJSONAccelerator/stargazers) - Generate Swift 5 model files from JSON with Codeable support.

**[back to top](#contributing-and-collaborating)**

### XML & HTML

*XML and HTML parsers, selectors and serializers.*

- [AEXML](https://github.com/tadija/AEXML) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/tadija/AEXML?style=flat)](https://github.com/tadija/AEXML/stargazers) - Simple and lightweight XML parser written in Swift.
- [Fuzi](https://github.com/cezheng/Fuzi) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/cezheng/Fuzi?style=flat)](https://github.com/cezheng/Fuzi/stargazers) - A fast & lightweight XML & HTML parser in Swift with XPath & CSS support.
- [HTMLKit](https://github.com/iabudiab/HTMLKit) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/iabudiab/HTMLKit?style=flat)](https://github.com/iabudiab/HTMLKit/stargazers) - An Objective-C framework for your everyday HTML needs.
- [Kanna](https://github.com/tid-kijyun/Kanna) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/tid-kijyun/Kanna?style=flat)](https://github.com/tid-kijyun/Kanna/stargazers)  - Kanna(鉋) is an XML/HTML parser for macOS/iOS.
- [Ono](https://github.com/mattt/Ono) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/mattt/Ono?style=flat)](https://github.com/mattt/Ono/stargazers) - A sensible way to deal with XML & HTML for iOS & macOS.
- [SwiftyXML](https://github.com/chenyunguiMilook/SwiftyXML) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/chenyunguiMilook/SwiftyXML?style=flat)](https://github.com/chenyunguiMilook/SwiftyXML/stargazers) - The most swifty way to deal with XML data in swift 4.
- [SwiftyXMLParser](https://github.com/yahoojapan/SwiftyXMLParser) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/yahoojapan/SwiftyXMLParser?style=flat)](https://github.com/yahoojapan/SwiftyXMLParser/stargazers) - Simple XML Parser implemented in Swift.
- [SWXMLHash](https://github.com/drmohundro/SWXMLHash) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/drmohundro/SWXMLHash?style=flat)](https://github.com/drmohundro/SWXMLHash/stargazers) - Simple XML parsing in Swift.
- [XMLCoder](https://github.com/MaxDesiatov/XMLCoder) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/MaxDesiatov/XMLCoder?style=flat)](https://github.com/MaxDesiatov/XMLCoder/stargazers) - Encoder & Decoder for XML using Swift's `Codable` protocols.
- [ZMarkupParser](https://github.com/ZhgChgLi/ZMarkupParser) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/ZhgChgLi/ZMarkupParser?style=flat)](https://github.com/ZhgChgLi/ZMarkupParser/stargazers) - Convert HTML strings into NSAttributedString with customized styles and tags.
