### Other Parsing

*Parsers for additional formats like YAML, INI and Markdown.*

- [CoreXLSX](https://github.com/MaxDesiatov/CoreXLSX) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/MaxDesiatov/CoreXLSX?style=flat)](https://github.com/MaxDesiatov/CoreXLSX/stargazers) - Excel spreadsheet (XLSX) format support in pure Swift.
- [CreateAPI](https://github.com/CreateAPI/CreateAPI) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/CreateAPI/CreateAPI?style=flat)](https://github.com/CreateAPI/CreateAPI/stargazers) - Delightful code generation for OpenAPI specs for Swift written in Swift.
- [Erik](https://github.com/phimage/Erik) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/phimage/Erik?style=flat)](https://github.com/phimage/Erik/stargazers) - Erik is an headless browser based on WebKit. An headless browser allow to run functional tests, to access and manipulate webpages using javascript.
- [FeedKit](https://github.com/nmdias/FeedKit) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/nmdias/FeedKit?style=flat)](https://github.com/nmdias/FeedKit/stargazers) - An RSS and Atom feed parser written in Swift.
- [NetNewsWire](https://github.com/Ranchero-Software/NetNewsWire) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/Ranchero-Software/NetNewsWire?style=flat)](https://github.com/Ranchero-Software/NetNewsWire/stargazers) - It’s a free and open-source feed reader for macOS and iOS.
- [SVGView](https://github.com/exyte/SVGView) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/exyte/SVGView?style=flat)](https://github.com/exyte/SVGView/stargazers) - SVG parser and renderer written in SwiftUI.
- [SwiftCssParser](https://github.com/100mango/SwiftCssParser) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/100mango/SwiftCssParser?style=flat)](https://github.com/100mango/SwiftCssParser/stargazers) - A Powerful , Extensible CSS Parser written in pure Swift.
- [URLEmbeddedView](https://github.com/marty-suzuki/URLEmbeddedView) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/marty-suzuki/URLEmbeddedView?style=flat)](https://github.com/marty-suzuki/URLEmbeddedView/stargazers) - Automatically caches the object that is confirmed the Open Graph Protocol, and displays it as URL embedded card.
- [URLPreview](https://github.com/itsmeichigo/URLPreview) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/itsmeichigo/URLPreview?style=flat)](https://github.com/itsmeichigo/URLPreview/stargazers) - An NSURL extension for showing preview info of webpages.
- [WKZombie](https://github.com/mkoehnke/WKZombie) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/mkoehnke/WKZombie?style=flat)](https://github.com/mkoehnke/WKZombie/stargazers) - WKZombie is a Swift framework for iOS/macOS to navigate within websites and collect data without the need of User Interface or API, also known as Headless browser. It can be used to run automated tests or manipulate websites using Javascript.

## Payments

*In-app purchase, subscription and payment gateway helpers.*

- [Braintree](https://www.braintreepayments.com) - Free payment processing on your first $50k. Requires Backend.
- [Caishen](https://github.com/prolificinteractive/Caishen) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/prolificinteractive/Caishen?style=flat)](https://github.com/prolificinteractive/Caishen/stargazers) - A Payment Card UI & Validator for iOS.
- [CreditCardForm-iOS](https://github.com/orazz/CreditCardForm-iOS) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/orazz/CreditCardForm-iOS?style=flat)](https://github.com/orazz/CreditCardForm-iOS/stargazers) - CreditCardForm is iOS framework that allows developers to create the UI which replicates an actual Credit Card.
- [FramesIos](https://github.com/checkout/frames-ios) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/checkout/frames-ios?style=flat)](https://github.com/checkout/frames-ios/stargazers) - Payment Form UI and Utilities in Swift.
- [iCard](https://github.com/eliakorkmaz/iCard) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/eliakorkmaz/iCard?style=flat)](https://github.com/eliakorkmaz/iCard/stargazers) - Bank Card Generator with Swift using SnapKit DSL.
- [merchantkit](https://github.com/benjaminmayo/merchantkit) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/benjaminmayo/merchantkit?style=flat)](https://github.com/benjaminmayo/merchantkit/stargazers) - A modern In-App Purchases management framework for iOS.
- [MFCard](https://github.com/MobileFirstInc/MFCard) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/MobileFirstInc/MFCard?style=flat)](https://github.com/MobileFirstInc/MFCard/stargazers) - Easily integrate Credit Card payments in iOS App / Customisable Card UI.
- [Moltin](https://www.moltin.com/developer/swift-ecommerce-sdk/) - Add eCommerce to your app with a simple SDK, so you can create a store and sell physical products, no backend required.
- [monza](https://github.com/gabrielgarza/monza) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/gabrielgarza/monza?style=flat)](https://github.com/gabrielgarza/monza/stargazers) - Ruby Gem for Rails - Easy iTunes In-App Purchase Receipt validation, including auto-renewable subscriptions.
- [PatronKit](https://github.com/MosheBerman/PatronKit) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/MosheBerman/PatronKit?style=flat)](https://github.com/MosheBerman/PatronKit/stargazers) - A framework to add patronage to your apps.
- [RMStore](https://github.com/robotmedia/RMStore) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/robotmedia/RMStore?style=flat)](https://github.com/robotmedia/RMStore/stargazers) - A lightweight iOS library for In-App Purchases.
- [Stripe](https://stripe.com) - Payment integration on your app with PAY. Suitable for people with low knowledge on Backend.
- [SwiftyStoreKit](https://github.com/bizz84/SwiftyStoreKit) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/bizz84/SwiftyStoreKit?style=flat)](https://github.com/bizz84/SwiftyStoreKit/stargazers) - Lightweight In App Purchases Swift framework for iOS 8.0+ and macOS 9.0+
- [TPInAppReceipt](https://github.com/tikhop/TPInAppReceipt) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/tikhop/TPInAppReceipt?style=flat)](https://github.com/tikhop/TPInAppReceipt/stargazers) - Reading and Validating In App Store Receipt.

**[back to top](#contributing-and-collaborating)**

## Permissions

*Unified APIs and UIs for requesting and managing iOS user permissions.*

- [ClusterPrePermissions](https://github.com/rsattar/ClusterPrePermissions) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/rsattar/ClusterPrePermissions?style=flat)](https://github.com/rsattar/ClusterPrePermissions/stargazers) - Reusable pre-permissions utility that lets developers ask users for access in their own dialog, before making the system-based request.
- [ISHPermissionKit](https://github.com/iosphere/ISHPermissionKit) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/iosphere/ISHPermissionKit?style=flat)](https://github.com/iosphere/ISHPermissionKit/stargazers) - A unified way for iOS apps to request user permissions.
- [PAPermissions](https://github.com/pascalbros/PAPermissions) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/pascalbros/PAPermissions?style=flat)](https://github.com/pascalbros/PAPermissions/stargazers) - A unified API to ask for permissions on iOS.
- [Permission](https://github.com/delba/Permission) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/delba/Permission?style=flat)](https://github.com/delba/Permission/stargazers) - A unified API to ask for permissions on iOS.
- [Proposer](https://github.com/nixzhu/Proposer) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/nixzhu/Proposer?style=flat)](https://github.com/nixzhu/Proposer/stargazers) - Make permission request easier (Supports Camera, Photos, Microphone, Contacts, Location).
- [SPPermissions](https://github.com/ivanvorobei/SPPermissions) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/ivanvorobei/SPPermissions?style=flat)](https://github.com/ivanvorobei/SPPermissions/stargazers) - Ask permissions on Swift. Available List, Dialog & Native interface. Can check state permission.

**[back to top](#contributing-and-collaborating)**

## Project setup

- [chairs](https://github.com/orta/chairs) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/orta/chairs?style=flat)](https://github.com/orta/chairs/stargazers) - Swap around your iOS Simulator Documents.
- [crafter](https://github.com/krzysztofzablocki/crafter) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/krzysztofzablocki/crafter?style=flat)](https://github.com/krzysztofzablocki/crafter/stargazers) - CLI that allows you to configure iOS project's template using custom DSL syntax, simple to use and quite powerful.
- [swift5-module-template](https://github.com/fulldecent/swift5-module-template) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/fulldecent/swift5-module-template?style=flat)](https://github.com/fulldecent/swift5-module-template/stargazers) - A starting point for any Swift 5 module that you want other people to include in their projects.
- [SwiftPlate](https://github.com/JohnSundell/SwiftPlate) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/JohnSundell/SwiftPlate?style=flat)](https://github.com/JohnSundell/SwiftPlate/stargazers) - Easily generate cross platform Swift framework projects from the command line.
- [Tuist](https://github.com/tuist/tuist) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/tuist/tuist?style=flat)](https://github.com/tuist/tuist/stargazers) - A tool to create, maintain and interact with Xcode projects at scale.
- [xcproj](https://github.com/tuist/xcodeproj) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/tuist/xcodeproj?style=flat)](https://github.com/tuist/xcodeproj/stargazers) - Read and update Xcode projects.

## Reactive Programming

*Reactive and functional reactive libraries for Swift and Objective-C.*

- [CwlSignal](https://github.com/mattgallagher/CwlSignal) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/mattgallagher/CwlSignal?style=flat)](https://github.com/mattgallagher/CwlSignal/stargazers) A Swift framework for reactive programming.
- [Hanson](https://github.com/blendle/Hanson) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/blendle/Hanson?style=flat)](https://github.com/blendle/Hanson/stargazers) - Lightweight observations and bindings in Swift, with support for KVO and NotificationCenter.
- [JASONETTE-iOS](https://github.com/Jasonette/JASONETTE-iOS) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/Jasonette/JASONETTE-iOS?style=flat)](https://github.com/Jasonette/JASONETTE-iOS/stargazers) - Native App over HTTP. Create your own native iOS app with nothing but JSON.
- [LightweightObservable](https://github.com/fxm90/LightweightObservable) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/fxm90/LightweightObservable?style=flat)](https://github.com/fxm90/LightweightObservable/stargazers) - A lightweight implementation of an observable sequence that you can subscribe to.
- [NSObject-Rx](https://github.com/RxSwiftCommunity/NSObject-Rx) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/RxSwiftCommunity/NSObject-Rx?style=flat)](https://github.com/RxSwiftCommunity/NSObject-Rx/stargazers) - Handy RxSwift extensions on NSObject, including rx_disposeBag.
- [Observable](https://github.com/roberthein/Observable) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/roberthein/Observable?style=flat)](https://github.com/roberthein/Observable/stargazers) - The easiest way to observe values in Swift.
- [OneWay](https://github.com/DevYeom/OneWay) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/DevYeom/OneWay?style=flat)](https://github.com/DevYeom/OneWay/stargazers) - A Swift library for state management with unidirectional data flow.
- [OpenCombine](https://github.com/broadwaylamb/OpenCombine) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/broadwaylamb/OpenCombine?style=flat)](https://github.com/broadwaylamb/OpenCombine/stargazers) — Open source implementation of Apple's Combine framework for processing values over time.
- [ReactiveCocoa](https://github.com/ReactiveCocoa/ReactiveCocoa) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/ReactiveCocoa/ReactiveCocoa?style=flat)](https://github.com/ReactiveCocoa/ReactiveCocoa/stargazers) - Streams of values over time.
- [ReactiveCoreData](https://github.com/apparentsoft/ReactiveCoreData) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/apparentsoft/ReactiveCoreData?style=flat)](https://github.com/apparentsoft/ReactiveCoreData/stargazers) - ReactiveCoreData (RCD) is an attempt to bring Core Data into the ReactiveCocoa (RAC) world.
- [ReactiveKit](https://github.com/DeclarativeHub/ReactiveKit) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/DeclarativeHub/ReactiveKit?style=flat)](https://github.com/DeclarativeHub/ReactiveKit/stargazers) - ReactiveKit is a collection of Swift frameworks for reactive and functional reactive programming.
- [ReactiveSwift](https://github.com/ReactiveCocoa/ReactiveSwift) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/ReactiveCocoa/ReactiveSwift?style=flat)](https://github.com/ReactiveCocoa/ReactiveSwift/stargazers) - Streams of values over time by ReactiveCocoa group.
- [ReactiveTask](https://github.com/Carthage/ReactiveTask) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/Carthage/ReactiveTask?style=flat)](https://github.com/Carthage/ReactiveTask/stargazers) - Flexible, stream-based abstraction for launching processes.
- [Reactor](https://github.com/ReactorSwift/Reactor) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/ReactorSwift/Reactor?style=flat)](https://github.com/ReactorSwift/Reactor/stargazers) - Unidirectional Data Flow using idiomatic Swift—inspired by Elm and Redux.
- [ReSwift](https://github.com/ReSwift/ReSwift) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/ReSwift/ReSwift?style=flat)](https://github.com/ReSwift/ReSwift/stargazers) - Unidirectional Data Flow in Swift - Inspired by Redux.
- [RxAlamofire](https://github.com/RxSwiftCommunity/RxAlamofire) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/RxSwiftCommunity/RxAlamofire?style=flat)](https://github.com/RxSwiftCommunity/RxAlamofire/stargazers) - RxSwift wrapper around the elegant HTTP networking in Swift Alamofire.
- [RxAnimated](https://github.com/RxSwiftCommunity/RxAnimated) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/RxSwiftCommunity/RxAnimated?style=flat)](https://github.com/RxSwiftCommunity/RxAnimated/stargazers) - Animated RxCocoa bindings.
- [RxBluetoothKit](https://github.com/Polidea/RxBluetoothKit) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/Polidea/RxBluetoothKit?style=flat)](https://github.com/Polidea/RxBluetoothKit/stargazers) - iOS & macOS Bluetooth library for RxSwift.
- [RxCoordinator](https://github.com/quickbirdstudios/XCoordinator) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/quickbirdstudios/XCoordinator?style=flat)](https://github.com/quickbirdstudios/XCoordinator/stargazers) -  Powerful navigation library for iOS based on the coordinator pattern.
- [RxCoreData](https://github.com/RxSwiftCommunity/RxCoreData) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/RxSwiftCommunity/RxCoreData?style=flat)](https://github.com/RxSwiftCommunity/RxCoreData/stargazers) - RxSwift extensions for Core Data.
- [RxGesture](https://github.com/RxSwiftCommunity/RxGesture) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/RxSwiftCommunity/RxGesture?style=flat)](https://github.com/RxSwiftCommunity/RxGesture/stargazers) - RxSwift reactive wrapper for view gestures.
- [RxKeyboard](https://github.com/RxSwiftCommunity/RxKeyboard) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/RxSwiftCommunity/RxKeyboard?style=flat)](https://github.com/RxSwiftCommunity/RxKeyboard/stargazers) - Reactive Keyboard in iOS.
- [RxMediaPicker](https://github.com/RxSwiftCommunity/RxMediaPicker) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/RxSwiftCommunity/RxMediaPicker?style=flat)](https://github.com/RxSwiftCommunity/RxMediaPicker/stargazers) - A reactive wrapper built around UIImagePickerController.
- [RxRealm](https://github.com/RxSwiftCommunity/RxRealm) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/RxSwiftCommunity/RxRealm?style=flat)](https://github.com/RxSwiftCommunity/RxRealm/stargazers) - Rx wrapper for Realm's collection types.
- [RxSwift](https://github.com/ReactiveX/RxSwift) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/ReactiveX/RxSwift?style=flat)](https://github.com/ReactiveX/RxSwift/stargazers) - Reactive Programming in Swift.
- [Verge](https://github.com/muukii/Verge) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/muukii/Verge?style=flat)](https://github.com/muukii/Verge/stargazers) - Verge is a faster and scalable state management library for UIKit and SwiftUI
- [VueFlux](https://github.com/ra1028/VueFlux) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/ra1028/VueFlux?style=flat)](https://github.com/ra1028/VueFlux/stargazers) - Unidirectional Data Flow State Management Architecture for Swift - Inspired by Vuex and Flux.

## Reflection

*Runtime reflection, mirroring and introspection helpers.*

- [EVReflection](https://github.com/evermeer/EVReflection) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/evermeer/EVReflection?style=flat)](https://github.com/evermeer/EVReflection/stargazers) - Reflection based JSON encoding and decoding. Including support for NSDictionary, NSCoding, Printable, Hashable and Equatable.
- [JSONNeverDie](https://github.com/johnlui/JSONNeverDie) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/johnlui/JSONNeverDie?style=flat)](https://github.com/johnlui/JSONNeverDie/stargazers) - Auto reflection tool from JSON to Model, user friendly JSON encoder / decoder, aims to never die.
- [Reflect](https://github.com/CharlinFeng/Reflect) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/CharlinFeng/Reflect?style=flat)](https://github.com/CharlinFeng/Reflect/stargazers) - Reflection, Dict2Model, Model2Dict, Archive.
- [Reflection](https://github.com/Zewo/Reflection) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/Zewo/Reflection?style=flat)](https://github.com/Zewo/Reflection/stargazers) - Reflection provides an API for advanced reflection at runtime including dynamic construction of types.
- [Runtime](https://github.com/wickwirew/Runtime) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/wickwirew/Runtime?style=flat)](https://github.com/wickwirew/Runtime/stargazers) - A Swift Runtime library for viewing type info, and the dynamic getting and setting of properties.
- [SwiftKVC](https://github.com/bradhilton/SwiftKVC) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/bradhilton/SwiftKVC?style=flat)](https://github.com/bradhilton/SwiftKVC/stargazers) - Key-Value Coding (KVC) for native Swift classes and structs.

**[back to top](#contributing-and-collaborating)**

- [AWS](https://github.com/aws-amplify/aws-sdk-ios) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/aws-amplify/aws-sdk-ios?style=flat)](https://github.com/aws-amplify/aws-sdk-ios/stargazers) Amazon Web Services Mobile SDK for iOS.

By Apple.

- [Firebase](https://firebase.google.com/docs/ios/setup) Mobile (and web) application development platform.
- [Google Analytics](https://developers.google.com/analytics/devguides/collection/ios/v3/) Google Analytics SDK for iOS.
- [Primer](https://www.goprimer.com/) - Easy SDK for creating personalized landing screens, signup, and login flows on a visual editor with built in a/b/n testing and analytics.
- [ResearchKit](https://github.com/ResearchKit/ResearchKit) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/ResearchKit/ResearchKit?style=flat)](https://github.com/ResearchKit/ResearchKit/stargazers) ResearchKit is an open source software framework that makes it easy to create apps for medical research or for other research projects.

## Security

*Tools and libraries for securing iOS apps, data and user credentials.*

- [BiometricAuthentication](https://github.com/rushisangani/BiometricAuthentication) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/rushisangani/BiometricAuthentication?style=flat)](https://github.com/rushisangani/BiometricAuthentication/stargazers) - Use Apple FaceID or TouchID authentication in your app using BiometricAuthentication.
- [cocoapods-keys](https://github.com/orta/cocoapods-keys) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/orta/cocoapods-keys?style=flat)](https://github.com/orta/cocoapods-keys/stargazers) - A key value store for storing environment and application keys.
- [LTHPasscodeViewController](https://github.com/rolandleth/LTHPasscodeViewController) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/rolandleth/LTHPasscodeViewController?style=flat)](https://github.com/rolandleth/LTHPasscodeViewController/stargazers) - An iOS passcode lockscreen replica (from Settings), with TouchID and simple (variable length) / complex support.
- [SecurePropertyStorage](https://github.com/alexruperez/SecurePropertyStorage) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/alexruperez/SecurePropertyStorage?style=flat)](https://github.com/alexruperez/SecurePropertyStorage/stargazers) - Helps you define secure storages for your properties using Swift property wrappers.
- [simple-touch](https://github.com/simple-machines/simple-touch) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/simple-machines/simple-touch?style=flat)](https://github.com/simple-machines/simple-touch/stargazers) - Very simple swift wrapper for Biometric Authentication Services (Touch ID) on iOS.
- [Smile-Lock](https://github.com/recruit-lifestyle/Smile-Lock) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/recruit-lifestyle/Smile-Lock?style=flat)](https://github.com/recruit-lifestyle/Smile-Lock/stargazers) - A library for make a beautiful Passcode Lock View.
- [SwiftPasscodeLock](https://github.com/yankodimitrov/SwiftPasscodeLock) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/yankodimitrov/SwiftPasscodeLock?style=flat)](https://github.com/yankodimitrov/SwiftPasscodeLock/stargazers) - An iOS passcode lock with TouchID authentication written in Swift.
- [TOPasscodeViewController](https://github.com/timoliver/TOPasscodeViewController) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/timoliver/TOPasscodeViewController?style=flat)](https://github.com/timoliver/TOPasscodeViewController/stargazers) - A modal passcode input and validation view controller for iOS.
- [zxcvbn-ios](https://github.com/dropbox/zxcvbn-ios) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/dropbox/zxcvbn-ios?style=flat)](https://github.com/dropbox/zxcvbn-ios/stargazers) - A realistic password strength estimator.

**[back to top](#contributing-and-collaborating)**

### Encryption

*Cryptography libraries for encryption, hashing and digital signatures.*

- [Arcane](https://github.com/onmyway133/Arcane) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/onmyway133/Arcane?style=flat)](https://github.com/onmyway133/Arcane/stargazers) - Lightweight wrapper around CommonCrypto in Swift.

- [IDZSwiftCommonCrypto](https://github.com/iosdevzone/IDZSwiftCommonCrypto) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/iosdevzone/IDZSwiftCommonCrypto?style=flat)](https://github.com/iosdevzone/IDZSwiftCommonCrypto/stargazers) - A wrapper for Apple's Common Crypto library written in Swift.

- [RNCryptor](https://github.com/RNCryptor/RNCryptor) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/RNCryptor/RNCryptor?style=flat)](https://github.com/RNCryptor/RNCryptor/stargazers) - CCCryptor (AES encryption) wrappers for iOS and Mac in Swift. -- For ObjC, see RNCryptor/RNCryptor-objc.
- [SipHash](https://github.com/attaswift/SipHash) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/attaswift/SipHash?style=flat)](https://github.com/attaswift/SipHash/stargazers) - Simple and secure hashing in Swift with the SipHash algorithm.
- [SwCrypt](https://github.com/soyersoyer/SwCrypt) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/soyersoyer/SwCrypt?style=flat)](https://github.com/soyersoyer/SwCrypt/stargazers) - RSA public/private key generation, RSA, AES encryption/decryption, RSA sign/verify in Swift with CommonCrypto in iOS and macOS.
- [swift-sodium](https://github.com/jedisct1/swift-sodium) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/jedisct1/swift-sodium?style=flat)](https://github.com/jedisct1/swift-sodium/stargazers) - Safe and easy to use crypto for iOS.
- [SwiftHash](https://github.com/onmyway133/SwiftHash) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/onmyway133/SwiftHash?style=flat)](https://github.com/onmyway133/SwiftHash/stargazers) - Hash in Swift.
- [SwiftyRSA](https://github.com/TakeScoop/SwiftyRSA) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/TakeScoop/SwiftyRSA?style=flat)](https://github.com/TakeScoop/SwiftyRSA/stargazers) - RSA public/private key encryption in Swift.
- [Themis](https://github.com/cossacklabs/themis) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/cossacklabs/themis?style=flat)](https://github.com/cossacklabs/themis/stargazers) - High-level crypto library, providing basic asymmetric encryption, secure messaging with forward secrecy and secure data storage, supports iOS/macOS, Android and different server side platforms.

### TDD / BDD

- [Kiwi](https://github.com/kiwi-bdd/Kiwi) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/kiwi-bdd/Kiwi?style=flat)](https://github.com/kiwi-bdd/Kiwi/stargazers) - A behavior-driven development library for iOS development.

Test your apps with fake network data and custom response time, response code and headers!

### Other Testing

*Snapshot testing, mocking, fuzzing and other testing utilities.*

- [Buildasaur](https://github.com/buildasaurs/Buildasaur) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/buildasaurs/Buildasaur?style=flat)](https://github.com/buildasaurs/Buildasaur/stargazers) - Automatic testing of your Pull Requests on GitHub and BitBucket using Xcode Server. Keep your team productive and safe. Get up and running in minutes.
- [Cuckoo](https://github.com/Brightify/Cuckoo) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/Brightify/Cuckoo?style=flat)](https://github.com/Brightify/Cuckoo/stargazers) - First boilerplate-free mocking framework for Swift.
- [DVR](https://github.com/venmo/DVR) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/venmo/DVR?style=flat)](https://github.com/venmo/DVR/stargazers) - Network testing for Swift.
- [ETTrace](https://github.com/EmergeTools/ETTrace) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/EmergeTools/ETTrace?style=flat)](https://github.com/EmergeTools/ETTrace/stargazers) - Locally measure performance of your app, without Xcode or Instruments.
- [Fakery](https://github.com/vadymmarkov/Fakery) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/vadymmarkov/Fakery?style=flat)](https://github.com/vadymmarkov/Fakery/stargazers) - Swift fake data generator.
- [iOS Snapshot Test Case](https://github.com/uber/ios-snapshot-test-case) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/uber/ios-snapshot-test-case?style=flat)](https://github.com/uber/ios-snapshot-test-case/stargazers) — Snapshot test your UIViews and CALayers on iOS and tvOS.
- [Kakapo](https://github.com/devlucky/Kakapo) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/devlucky/Kakapo?style=flat)](https://github.com/devlucky/Kakapo/stargazers) - Dynamically Mock server behaviors and responses in Swift.
- [MirrorDiffKit](https://github.com/Kuniwak/MirrorDiffKit) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/Kuniwak/MirrorDiffKit?style=flat)](https://github.com/Kuniwak/MirrorDiffKit/stargazers) - Pretty diff between any structs or classes.
- [Mockingbird](https://github.com/Farfetch/mockingbird) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/Farfetch/mockingbird?style=flat)](https://github.com/Farfetch/mockingbird/stargazers) - Simplify software testing, by easily mocking any system using HTTP/HTTPS, allowing a team to test and develop against a service that is not complete, unstable or just to reproduce planned cases.
- [Mockingjay](https://github.com/kylef/Mockingjay) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/kylef/Mockingjay?style=flat)](https://github.com/kylef/Mockingjay/stargazers) - An elegant library for stubbing HTTP requests with ease in Swift.
- [Mockit](https://github.com/sabirvirtuoso/Mockit) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/sabirvirtuoso/Mockit?style=flat)](https://github.com/sabirvirtuoso/Mockit/stargazers) - A simple mocking framework for Swift, inspired by the famous Mockito for Java.
- [OCMock](https://ocmock.org/) - Mock objects for Objective-C.
- [second_curtain](https://github.com/ashfurrow/second_curtain) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/ashfurrow/second_curtain?style=flat)](https://github.com/ashfurrow/second_curtain/stargazers) - Upload failing iOS snapshot tests cases to S3.

## Text

OAStackView aims at replicating all the features in UIStackView.

- [Pageboy](https://github.com/uias/Pageboy) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/uias/Pageboy?style=flat)](https://github.com/uias/Pageboy/stargazers) - A simple, highly informative page view controller.
- [PageController](https://github.com/hirohisa/PageController) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/hirohisa/PageController?style=flat)](https://github.com/hirohisa/PageController/stargazers) - Infinite paging controller, scrolling through contents and title bar scrolls with a delay.
- [Pages](https://github.com/hyperoslo/Pages) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/hyperoslo/Pages?style=flat)](https://github.com/hyperoslo/Pages/stargazers) - UIPageViewController made simple.
- [Pulley](https://github.com/52inc/Pulley) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/52inc/Pulley?style=flat)](https://github.com/52inc/Pulley/stargazers) - A library to imitate the iOS 10 Maps UI.
- [RKNotificationHub](https://github.com/cwRichardKim/RKNotificationHub) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/cwRichardKim/RKNotificationHub?style=flat)](https://github.com/cwRichardKim/RKNotificationHub/stargazers) - Make any UIView a full fledged notification center.
- [SCTrelloNavigation](https://github.com/SergioChan/SCTrelloNavigation) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/SergioChan/SCTrelloNavigation?style=flat)](https://github.com/SergioChan/SCTrelloNavigation/stargazers) - An iOS native implementation of a Trello Animated Navigation. 
- [SegmentedProgressBar](https://github.com/D-32/SegmentedProgressBar) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/D-32/SegmentedProgressBar?style=flat)](https://github.com/D-32/SegmentedProgressBar/stargazers) - Snapchat / Instagram Stories style animated indicator.

Customisable transform and duration.

### Label

*Enhanced UILabel replacements and text-display utilities.*

- [ActiveLabel.swift](https://github.com/optonaut/ActiveLabel.swift) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/optonaut/ActiveLabel.swift?style=flat)](https://github.com/optonaut/ActiveLabel.swift/stargazers) - UILabel drop-in replacement supporting Hashtags (#), Mentions (@) and URLs (http://) written in Swift
- [CountdownLabel](https://github.com/suzuki-0000/CountdownLabel) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/suzuki-0000/CountdownLabel?style=flat)](https://github.com/suzuki-0000/CountdownLabel/stargazers) - Simple countdown UILabel with morphing animation, and some useful function.
- [GlitchLabel](https://github.com/kciter/GlitchLabel) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/kciter/GlitchLabel?style=flat)](https://github.com/kciter/GlitchLabel/stargazers) - Glitching UILabel for iOS.
- [LTMorphingLabel](https://github.com/lexrus/LTMorphingLabel) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/lexrus/LTMorphingLabel?style=flat)](https://github.com/lexrus/LTMorphingLabel/stargazers) - Graceful morphing effects for UILabel written in Swift.
- [MZTimerLabel](https://github.com/mineschan/MZTimerLabel) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/mineschan/MZTimerLabel?style=flat)](https://github.com/mineschan/MZTimerLabel/stargazers) - A handy class for iOS to use UILabel as a countdown timer or stopwatch just like in Apple Clock App.
- [NumberMorphView](https://github.com/me-abhinav/NumberMorphView) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/me-abhinav/NumberMorphView?style=flat)](https://github.com/me-abhinav/NumberMorphView/stargazers) - A label view for displaying numbers which can transition or animate using a technique called number tweening or number morphing.
- [Preloader.Ophiuchus](https://github.com/Yalantis/Preloader.Ophiuchus) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/Yalantis/Preloader.Ophiuchus?style=flat)](https://github.com/Yalantis/Preloader.Ophiuchus/stargazers) - Custom Label to apply animations on whole text or letters.
- [RQShineLabel](https://github.com/zipme/RQShineLabel) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/zipme/RQShineLabel?style=flat)](https://github.com/zipme/RQShineLabel/stargazers) - Secret app like text animation
- [STULabel](https://github.com/stephan-tolksdorf/STULabel) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/stephan-tolksdorf/STULabel?style=flat)](https://github.com/stephan-tolksdorf/STULabel/stargazers) -  A label view that's faster than UILabel and supports asynchronous rendering, links with UIDragInteraction, very flexible text truncation, Auto Layout, UIAccessibility and more.
- [THLabel](https://github.com/tobihagemann/THLabel) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/tobihagemann/THLabel?style=flat)](https://github.com/tobihagemann/THLabel/stargazers) - UILabel subclass, which additionally allows shadow blur, inner shadow, stroke text and fill gradient.
- [TOMSMorphingLabel](https://github.com/tomknig/TOMSMorphingLabel) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/tomknig/TOMSMorphingLabel?style=flat)](https://github.com/tomknig/TOMSMorphingLabel/stargazers) - Configurable morphing transitions between text values of a label.
- [TriLabelView](https://github.com/mukeshthawani/TriLabelView) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/mukeshthawani/TriLabelView?style=flat)](https://github.com/mukeshthawani/TriLabelView/stargazers) - A triangle shaped corner label view for iOS written in Swift.
- [TTTAttributedLabel](https://github.com/TTTAttributedLabel/TTTAttributedLabel) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/TTTAttributedLabel/TTTAttributedLabel?style=flat)](https://github.com/TTTAttributedLabel/TTTAttributedLabel/stargazers) - A drop-in replacement for UILabel that supports attributes, data detectors, links, and more
- [UICountingLabel](https://github.com/dataxpress/UICountingLabel/) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/dataxpress/UICountingLabel/?style=flat)](https://github.com/dataxpress/UICountingLabel//stargazers) - Adds animated counting support to UILabel.
- [ZCAnimatedLabel](https://github.com/overboming/ZCAnimatedLabel) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/overboming/ZCAnimatedLabel?style=flat)](https://github.com/overboming/ZCAnimatedLabel/stargazers) - UILabel replacement with fine-grain appear/disappear animation

**[back to top](#contributing-and-collaborating)**

### Login

*Pre-built login UIs and authentication flows.*

- [Cely](https://github.com/cely-tools/Cely) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/cely-tools/Cely?style=flat)](https://github.com/cely-tools/Cely/stargazers) - Plug-n-Play login framework written in Swift.
- [LFLoginController](https://github.com/awesome-labs/LFLoginController) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/awesome-labs/LFLoginController?style=flat)](https://github.com/awesome-labs/LFLoginController/stargazers) - Customizable login screen, written in Swift.
- [LoginKit](https://github.com/IcaliaLabs/LoginKit) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/IcaliaLabs/LoginKit?style=flat)](https://github.com/IcaliaLabs/LoginKit/stargazers) - LoginKit is a quick and easy way to add a Login/Signup UX to your iOS app.

### Menu

- [AirBar](https://github.com/uptechteam/AirBar) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/uptechteam/AirBar?style=flat)](https://github.com/uptechteam/AirBar/stargazers) - UIScrollView driven expandable menu written in Swift 3.

- [BTNavigationDropdownMenu](https://github.com/PhamBaTho/BTNavigationDropdownMenu) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/PhamBaTho/BTNavigationDropdownMenu?style=flat)](https://github.com/PhamBaTho/BTNavigationDropdownMenu/stargazers) - The elegant dropdown menu, written in Swift, appears underneath navigation bar to display a list of related items when a user click on the navigation title.
- [CategorySliderView](https://github.com/cemolcay/CategorySliderView) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/cemolcay/CategorySliderView?style=flat)](https://github.com/cemolcay/CategorySliderView/stargazers) - slider view for choosing categories. add any UIView type as category item view. Fully customisable

- [DropDown](https://github.com/AssistoLab/DropDown) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/AssistoLab/DropDown?style=flat)](https://github.com/AssistoLab/DropDown/stargazers) - A Material Design drop down for iOS

### Navigation Bar

- [KDInteractiveNavigationController](https://github.com/kingiol/KDInteractiveNavigationController) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/kingiol/KDInteractiveNavigationController?style=flat)](https://github.com/kingiol/KDInteractiveNavigationController/stargazers) - A UINavigationController subclass that support pop interactive UINavigationbar with hidden or show.

- [RainbowNavigation](https://github.com/DanisFabric/RainbowNavigation) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/DanisFabric/RainbowNavigation?style=flat)](https://github.com/DanisFabric/RainbowNavigation/stargazers) - An easy way to change backgroundColor of UINavigationBar when Push & Pop
- [TONavigationBar](https://github.com/TimOliver/TONavigationBar) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/TimOliver/TONavigationBar?style=flat)](https://github.com/TimOliver/TONavigationBar/stargazers) - A simple subclass that adds the ability to set the navigation bar background to 'clear' and gradually transition it visibly back in, similar to the effect in the iOS Music app.

### Popup

*Popups, modals, bottom sheets and overlay components.*

- [AZDialogViewController](https://github.com/Minitour/AZDialogViewController) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/Minitour/AZDialogViewController?style=flat)](https://github.com/Minitour/AZDialogViewController/stargazers) - A highly customizable alert dialog controller that mimics Snapchat's alert dialog.
- [FFPopup](https://github.com/JonyFang/FFPopup) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/JonyFang/FFPopup?style=flat)](https://github.com/JonyFang/FFPopup/stargazers) - ⛩FFPopup is a lightweight library for presenting custom views as a popup.

#### Collection View Layout

*Custom collection view layouts: waterfall, circular, tag-cloud and more.*

- [AZSafariCollectionViewLayout](https://github.com/AfrozZaheer/AZSafariCollectionViewLayout) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/AfrozZaheer/AZSafariCollectionViewLayout?style=flat)](https://github.com/AfrozZaheer/AZSafariCollectionViewLayout/stargazers) - AZSafariCollectionViewLayout is replica of safari browser history page layout. very easy to use, IBInspectable are given for easy integration.
- [BouncyLayout](https://github.com/roberthein/BouncyLayout) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/roberthein/BouncyLayout?style=flat)](https://github.com/roberthein/BouncyLayout/stargazers) - BouncyLayout is a collection view layout that makes your cells bounce.
- [CenteredCollectionView](https://github.com/BenEmdon/CenteredCollectionView) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/BenEmdon/CenteredCollectionView?style=flat)](https://github.com/BenEmdon/CenteredCollectionView/stargazers) - A lightweight UICollectionViewLayout that _'pages'_ and centers it's cells 🎡 written in Swift.
- [CHTCollectionViewWaterfallLayout](https://github.com/chiahsien/CHTCollectionViewWaterfallLayout) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/chiahsien/CHTCollectionViewWaterfallLayout?style=flat)](https://github.com/chiahsien/CHTCollectionViewWaterfallLayout/stargazers) - The waterfall (i.e., Pinterest-like) layout for UICollectionView.
- [CollectionViewSlantedLayout](https://github.com/yacir/CollectionViewSlantedLayout) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/yacir/CollectionViewSlantedLayout?style=flat)](https://github.com/yacir/CollectionViewSlantedLayout/stargazers) - UICollectionViewLayout with slanted content
- [mosaic-layout](https://github.com/vinnyoodles/mosaic-layout) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/vinnyoodles/mosaic-layout?style=flat)](https://github.com/vinnyoodles/mosaic-layout/stargazers) - A mosaic collection view layout inspired by Lightbox's Algorithm, written in Swift
- [SquareMosaicLayout](https://github.com/iwheelbuy/SquareMosaicLayout) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/iwheelbuy/SquareMosaicLayout?style=flat)](https://github.com/iwheelbuy/SquareMosaicLayout/stargazers) - An extandable mosaic UICollectionViewLayout with a focus on extremely flexible customizations
- [Swinflate](https://github.com/VladIacobIonut/Swinflate) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/VladIacobIonut/Swinflate?style=flat)](https://github.com/VladIacobIonut/Swinflate/stargazers) -  A bunch of layouts providing light and seamless experiences in your CollectionView.
- [TLLayoutTransitioning](https://github.com/SwiftKickMobile/TLLayoutTransitioning) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/SwiftKickMobile/TLLayoutTransitioning?style=flat)](https://github.com/SwiftKickMobile/TLLayoutTransitioning/stargazers) - Enhanced transitioning between UICollectionView layouts in iOS.
- [UICollectionViewSplitLayout](https://github.com/yahoojapan/UICollectionViewSplitLayout) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/yahoojapan/UICollectionViewSplitLayout?style=flat)](https://github.com/yahoojapan/UICollectionViewSplitLayout/stargazers) - UICollectionViewSplitLayout makes collection view more responsive.

Powered by Swift.

## WebSocket

*WebSocket client libraries for real-time communication on iOS.*

- [socket.io-client-swift](https://github.com/socketio/socket.io-client-swift) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/socketio/socket.io-client-swift?style=flat)](https://github.com/socketio/socket.io-client-swift/stargazers) - Socket.IO-client for iOS/macOS.
- [SocketRocket](https://github.com/facebook/SocketRocket) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/facebook/SocketRocket?style=flat)](https://github.com/facebook/SocketRocket/stargazers) - A conforming Objective-C WebSocket client library.
- [Socks](https://github.com/vapor-community/sockets) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/vapor-community/sockets?style=flat)](https://github.com/vapor-community/sockets/stargazers) - Pure-Swift Sockets: TCP, UDP; Client, Server; Linux, macOS.
- [Starscream](https://github.com/daltoniam/Starscream) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/daltoniam/Starscream?style=flat)](https://github.com/daltoniam/Starscream/stargazers) - Websockets in swift for iOS and macOS.
- [Swift-ActionCableClient](https://github.com/danielrhodes/Swift-ActionCableClient) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/danielrhodes/Swift-ActionCableClient?style=flat)](https://github.com/danielrhodes/Swift-ActionCableClient/stargazers) - ActionCable is a new WebSocket server being released with Rails 5 which makes it easy to add real-time features to your app.
- [SwiftSocket](https://github.com/swiftsocket/SwiftSocket) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/swiftsocket/SwiftSocket?style=flat)](https://github.com/swiftsocket/SwiftSocket/stargazers) - simple socket library for apple swift lang.

## Tools

*Command-line utilities, code generators and helper tools for iOS development.*

- [abandoned-strings](https://github.com/ijoshsmith/abandoned-strings) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/ijoshsmith/abandoned-strings?style=flat)](https://github.com/ijoshsmith/abandoned-strings/stargazers) - Command line program that detects unused resource strings in an iOS or macOS application.
- [AppDevKit](https://github.com/yahoo/AppDevKit) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/yahoo/AppDevKit?style=flat)](https://github.com/yahoo/AppDevKit/stargazers) - AppDevKit is an iOS development library that provides developers with useful features to fulfill their everyday iOS app development needs.
- [appledoc](https://github.com/tomaz/appledoc) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/tomaz/appledoc?style=flat)](https://github.com/tomaz/appledoc/stargazers) - ObjectiveC code Apple style documentation set generator.
- [AssetChecker 👮](https://github.com/freshOS/AssetChecker) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/freshOS/AssetChecker?style=flat)](https://github.com/freshOS/AssetChecker/stargazers) - Keeps your Assets.xcassets files clean and emits warnings when something is suspicious.
- [Attabench](https://github.com/attaswift/Attabench) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/attaswift/Attabench?style=flat)](https://github.com/attaswift/Attabench/stargazers) - Microbenchmarking app for Swift with nice log-log plots.
- [AVXCAssets-Generator](https://github.com/angelvasa/AVXCAssets-Generator) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/angelvasa/AVXCAssets-Generator?style=flat)](https://github.com/angelvasa/AVXCAssets-Generator/stargazers) - AVXCAssets Generator takes path for your assets images and creates appiconset and imageset for you in just one click.
- [Blade](https://github.com/jondot/blade) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/jondot/blade?style=flat)](https://github.com/jondot/blade/stargazers) - Generate Xcode image catalogs for iOS / macOS app icons, universal images, and more.
- [BuildTimeAnalyzer](https://github.com/RobertGummesson/BuildTimeAnalyzer-for-Xcode) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/RobertGummesson/BuildTimeAnalyzer-for-Xcode?style=flat)](https://github.com/RobertGummesson/BuildTimeAnalyzer-for-Xcode/stargazers) - Build Time Analyzer for Swift.
- [Cichlid](https://github.com/dealforest/Cichlid) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/dealforest/Cichlid?style=flat)](https://github.com/dealforest/Cichlid/stargazers) - automatically delete the current project's DerivedData directories.
- [Cutter](https://cutter.albemala.me/) - A tool to generate iOS Launch Images (Splash Screens) for all screen sizes starting from a single template.
- [Duration](https://github.com/SwiftStudies/Duration) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/SwiftStudies/Duration?style=flat)](https://github.com/SwiftStudies/Duration/stargazers) - A simple Swift package for measuring and reporting the time taken for operations.
- [Ecno](https://github.com/xmartlabs/Ecno) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/xmartlabs/Ecno?style=flat)](https://github.com/xmartlabs/Ecno/stargazers) - Ecno is a task state manager built on top of UserDefaults in pure Swift 3.
- [fastlane-plugin-appicon](https://github.com/fastlane-community/fastlane-plugin-appicon) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/fastlane-community/fastlane-plugin-appicon?style=flat)](https://github.com/fastlane-community/fastlane-plugin-appicon/stargazers) - Generate required icon sizes and iconset from a master application icon.
- [FBSimulatorControl](https://github.com/facebook/idb) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/facebook/idb?style=flat)](https://github.com/facebook/idb/stargazers) - A macOS library for managing and manipulating iOS Simulators
- [FengNiao](https://github.com/onevcat/FengNiao) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/onevcat/FengNiao?style=flat)](https://github.com/onevcat/FengNiao/stargazers) - A command line tool for cleaning unused resources in Xcode.
- [GDPerformanceView-Swift](https://github.com/dani-gavrilov/GDPerformanceView-Swift) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/dani-gavrilov/GDPerformanceView-Swift?style=flat)](https://github.com/dani-gavrilov/GDPerformanceView-Swift/stargazers) - Shows FPS, CPU usage, app and iOS versions above the status bar and report FPS and CPU usage via delegate.
- [GetUniversal.link](https://getuniversal.link/) - Free Universal Link & Apple App Site Association testing tool.
- [IBM Swift Sandbox](https://swift.sandbox.bluemix.net) - The IBM Swift Sandbox is an interactive website that lets you write Swift code and execute it in a server environment – on top of Linux!
- [infer](https://github.com/facebook/infer) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/facebook/infer?style=flat)](https://github.com/facebook/infer/stargazers) - A static analyzer for Java, C and Objective-C.

- [Kin](https://github.com/Karumi/Kin) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/Karumi/Kin?style=flat)](https://github.com/Karumi/Kin/stargazers) - Have you ever found yourself undoing a merge due to a broken Xcode build? Then Kin is your tool. It will parse your project configuration file and detect errors.
- [Laurine](https://github.com/JiriTrecak/Laurine) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/JiriTrecak/Laurine?style=flat)](https://github.com/JiriTrecak/Laurine/stargazers) - Laurine - Localization code generator written in Swift. Sweet!
- [LicensePlist](https://github.com/mono0926/LicensePlist) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/mono0926/LicensePlist?style=flat)](https://github.com/mono0926/LicensePlist/stargazers) - A license list generator of all your dependencies for iOS applications.
- [LifetimeTracker](https://github.com/krzysztofzablocki/LifetimeTracker) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/krzysztofzablocki/LifetimeTracker?style=flat)](https://github.com/krzysztofzablocki/LifetimeTracker/stargazers) - Find retain cycles / memory leaks sooner.

- [nef](https://github.com/bow-swift/nef) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/bow-swift/nef?style=flat)](https://github.com/bow-swift/nef/stargazers) - A set of command line tools for Xcode Playground: lets you have compile-time verification of your documentation written as Xcode Playgrounds, generates markdown files, integration with Jekyll for building microsites and Carbon to export code snippets.
- [Nomad](https://nomad-cli.com) - Suite of command line utilities & libraries for sending APNs, create & distribute `.ipa`, verify In-App-Purchase receipt and more.
- [Pecker](https://github.com/woshiccm/Pecker) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/woshiccm/Pecker?style=flat)](https://github.com/woshiccm/Pecker/stargazers) - CodePecker is a tool to detect unused code.

## Xcode

*Extensions, themes and other enhancements for Xcode.*

### Extensions

*Xcode source editor and project extensions.*

* [CleanClosureXcode](https://github.com/BalestraPatrick/CleanClosureXcode) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/BalestraPatrick/CleanClosureXcode?style=flat)](https://github.com/BalestraPatrick/CleanClosureXcode/stargazers) - An Xcode Source Editor extension to clean the closure syntax.
* [xTextHandler](https://github.com/cyanzhong/xTextHandler) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/cyanzhong/xTextHandler?style=flat)](https://github.com/cyanzhong/xTextHandler/stargazers) - Xcode Source Editor Extension Toolset (Plugins for Xcode 8).
* [SwiftInitializerGenerator](https://github.com/Bouke/SwiftInitializerGenerator) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/Bouke/SwiftInitializerGenerator?style=flat)](https://github.com/Bouke/SwiftInitializerGenerator/stargazers) - Xcode 8 Source Code Extension to Generate Swift Initializers.
* [XcodeEquatableGenerator](https://github.com/sergdort/XcodeEquatableGenerator) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/sergdort/XcodeEquatableGenerator?style=flat)](https://github.com/sergdort/XcodeEquatableGenerator/stargazers) - Xcode 8 Source Code Extension will generate conformance to Swift Equatable protocol based on type and fields selection.
* [Import](https://github.com/markohlebar/Import) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/markohlebar/Import?style=flat)](https://github.com/markohlebar/Import/stargazers) - Xcode extension for adding imports from anywhere in the code.
* [Mark](https://github.com/velyan/Mark) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/velyan/Mark?style=flat)](https://github.com/velyan/Mark/stargazers) - Xcode extension for generating MARK comments.
* [XShared](https://github.com/Otbivnoe/XShared) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/Otbivnoe/XShared?style=flat)](https://github.com/Otbivnoe/XShared/stargazers) - Xcode extension which allows you copying the code with special formatting quotes for social (Slack, Telegram).
* [XGist](https://github.com/Bunn/Xgist) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/Bunn/Xgist?style=flat)](https://github.com/Bunn/Xgist/stargazers) - Xcode extension which allows you to send your text selection or entire file to GitHub's Gist and automatically copy the Gist URL into your Clipboard.
* [Swiftify](https://swiftify.com/) - Objective-C to Swift online code converter and Xcode extension.
* [DocumenterXcode](https://github.com/serhii-londar/DocumenterXcode) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/serhii-londar/DocumenterXcode?style=flat)](https://github.com/serhii-londar/DocumenterXcode/stargazers) - Attempt to give a new life for VVDocumenter-Xcode as source editor extension.
* [Snowonder](https://github.com/Karetski/Snowonder) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/Karetski/Snowonder?style=flat)](https://github.com/Karetski/Snowonder/stargazers) - Magical import declarations formatter for Xcode.
* [XVim2](https://github.com/XVimProject/XVim2) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/XVimProject/XVim2?style=flat)](https://github.com/XVimProject/XVim2/stargazers) - Vim key-bindings for Xcode 9.
* [Comment Spell Checker](https://github.com/velyan/Comment-Spell-Checker) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/velyan/Comment-Spell-Checker?style=flat)](https://github.com/velyan/Comment-Spell-Checker/stargazers) - Xcode extension for spell checking and auto correcting code comments.
* [nef](https://github.com/bow-swift/nef-plugin) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/bow-swift/nef-plugin?style=flat)](https://github.com/bow-swift/nef-plugin/stargazers) - This Xcode extension enables you to make a code selection and export it to a snippets. Available on Mac AppStore.

- [Solarized-Dark-for-Xcode](https://github.com/ArtSabintsev/Solarized-Dark-for-Xcode/) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/ArtSabintsev/Solarized-Dark-for-Xcode/?style=flat)](https://github.com/ArtSabintsev/Solarized-Dark-for-Xcode//stargazers) - Solarized Dark Theme for Xcode 5.
- [WWDC2016 Xcode Color Scheme](https://github.com/cargath/WWDC2016-Xcode-Color-Scheme) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/cargath/WWDC2016-Xcode-Color-Scheme?style=flat)](https://github.com/cargath/WWDC2016-Xcode-Color-Scheme/stargazers) - A color scheme for Xcode based on the WWDC 2016 invitation.
- [Xcode themes list](https://github.com/hdoria/xcode-themes) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/hdoria/xcode-themes?style=flat)](https://github.com/hdoria/xcode-themes/stargazers) - Color themes for Xcode.

**[back to top](#contributing-and-collaborating)**


### Other Xcode

*Additional Xcode plugins, helpers and utilities.*

- [awesome-xcode-scripts](https://github.com/aashishtamsya/awesome-xcode-scripts) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/aashishtamsya/awesome-xcode-scripts?style=flat)](https://github.com/aashishtamsya/awesome-xcode-scripts/stargazers) - A curated list of useful xcode scripts.
- [SBShortcutMenuSimulator](https://github.com/DeskConnect/SBShortcutMenuSimulator) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/DeskConnect/SBShortcutMenuSimulator?style=flat)](https://github.com/DeskConnect/SBShortcutMenuSimulator/stargazers) - 3D Touch shortcuts in the Simulator.
- [Swift Macros 🚀](https://github.com/krzysztofzablocki/Swift-Macros) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/krzysztofzablocki/Swift-Macros?style=flat)](https://github.com/krzysztofzablocki/Swift-Macros/stargazers) - A curated list of community-created Macros and associated learning resources.
- [Synx](https://github.com/venmo/synx) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/venmo/synx?style=flat)](https://github.com/venmo/synx/stargazers) - A command-line tool that reorganizes your Xcode project folder to match your Xcode groups.
- [Xcode Developer Disk Images](https://github.com/haikieu/xcode-developer-disk-image-all-platforms) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/haikieu/xcode-developer-disk-image-all-platforms?style=flat)](https://github.com/haikieu/xcode-developer-disk-image-all-platforms/stargazers) - Xcode Developer Disk Images is needed when you want to put your build to the device, however sometimes your Xcode is not updated with the latest Disk Images, you could find them here for convenience.
- [Xcode Keymap for Visual Studio Code](https://marketplace.visualstudio.com/items?itemName=stevemoser.xcode-keybindings) - This extension ports popular Xcode keyboard shortcuts to Visual Studio Code.

**[back to top](#contributing-and-collaborating)**
